Japanese Military

Reform Plan for Manchukuo Organizations

(Nanjing) Nagata, Director of the Army Ministry's Military Affairs Bureau, visited Vice-Minister Pingkami of the Colonial Affairs Ministry on the 4th to present and explain the Army Minister's plan to reform the organizations in Manchukuo. Today, he will visit Vice-Minister Shigemitsu of the Foreign Ministry to provide the same explanation. The contents of the plan are as follows: First, the basic policy: (1) Respect the independence of Manchukuo and promote its rapid development. The reform of the organizations in Manchukuo cannot become colonial. (2) According to what is clearly stated in the Japan-Manchukuo Protocol, the relationship between Japan and Manchukuo is inseparable. Therefore, the relationship between the Empire and Manchukuo is different from the relationship between the Empire and other independent countries. (3) The policy towards Manchukuo is an important national policy of the Empire and cannot be monopolized by one department. Second, reform the organizations in Manchukuo: (1) The Chokunin-rank Governor-General of the Kwantung Leased Territory is the governor of the Kwantung Leased Territory and is placed under the command of the Ambassador Plenipotentiary. (2) The Ambassador Plenipotentiary, because of the special relationship between the two countries, is not a pure diplomat. Except for diplomatic issues, before the extraterritoriality is abolished, the police affairs, special companies such as the South Manchuria Railway, and the supervision and control of the Japanese in Manchukuo are all under his jurisdiction. (3) Manchukuo is an independent country, so guidance is not exercised over it. (4) From the perspective of the actual situation of Manchukuo's security and the joint defense of Japan and Manchukuo, the Ambassador Plenipotentiary concurrently serves as the Commander of the Kwantung Army. (5) In order to materialize the spirit of the Japan-Manchukuo Protocol, the Commander of the Kwantung Army maintains the current relationship with Manchukuo. (6) Conclude treaties such as the Japan-Manchukuo Economic Alliance. (7) In order to implement this treaty, a Japan-Manchukuo Economic Conference is established on a regular basis. The results of the negotiations are reported to the governments of both countries for implementation. (8) The Kwantung Army Special Service Department and other organizations merge with the Japan-Manchukuo Economic Conference. (9) The embassy's police affairs agencies and the Kwantung Military Police are placed under the command of the Commander of the Kwantung Military Police. (10) After the Kwantung Leased Territory is abolished, a new agency at the counselor level is established in the embassy to manage the supervision of special companies in Manchukuo under the jurisdiction of the Ambassador Plenipotentiary. Third, the reform of the internal affairs agencies: (1) Regarding the Commander of the Army's national defense military affairs, the German Parliament convenes.

Commemorating President Hindenburg

Hitler Praises the Hero of Tannenberg

But Not a Word About the Current Situation

(Berlin) At exactly 12 noon today, the Diet convened in the Kroll Opera House. The crowd was extremely crowded. Speaker Goering stood up and declared in his clear and sorrowful tone, "I now announce the opening of the meeting to commemorate the late President Hindenburg. I ask everyone to stand in silence to express our condolences." After the speech, the Diet was silent for one minute. (6th National Electric)

(Berlin) Prime Minister Hitler gave a speech in the Diet today to commemorate the hero of Tannenberg, praising the late President Hindenburg. Hitler's speech lasted from 12:10 p.m. to 12:25 p.m., detailing Hindenburg's achievements, saying that the late President's fame would be forever immortalized in German history. Hitler also read out the official report of the Battle of Tannenberg, calling the Battle of Tannenberg the greatest war in history. This great achievement will be passed down forever along with this great fame. He also said that if our politics can keep pace with our country's military affairs, Germany will not fear foreign aggression. Marshal Hindenburg is the one who turned Germany from danger to safety. (6th National Electric)

(Berlin) At noon today, the crowd in front of the Berlin Church was rarely seen. The church doors had to be temporarily closed until 1:30 p.m., and then the Chief Pastor Dr. Mueller led a memorial prayer for the late President Hindenburg. (5th National Electric)

2,000 People in the Diet

Listen to Hitler's Speech

The Deposed Crown Prince Arrived the Earliest

The Diplomatic Corps Box Was Completely Full

(Berlin) The German House of Representatives convened in the Kroll Theater today. The new President and Prime Minister Hitler attended the meeting and gave a speech praising the late President Hindenburg's great achievements. 2,000 people listened, and the deposed Crown Prince was also among them. The deposed Crown Prince arrived quite early. Defense Minister General von Blomberg warmly welcomed him. All the cabinet members attended the meeting. Many cabinet members and all the members of the Diet wore brown shirts. The diplomatic corps box was completely full. Hitler wore a brown uniform, with a black gauze tied around his arm. He stood next to Hindenburg's son, Colonel Hindenburg, and spoke. Unexpectedly, Hitler did not say a word about the current political situation and the position of president. His speech only lasted 15 minutes, praising the late President's war achievements in the Prussian-Austrian War and the Franco-Prussian War, and his service in the army during peacetime. He then said that Hindenburg retired to his hometown in 1911. Later, the former Emperor appointed him to command the eastern border and defeat the Russian army, thus saving Germany from destruction. It was not until then that Marshal Hindenburg's fame was heard all over the world. A catchphrase in Hitler's speech was: "Marshal Hindenburg is not dead. He is still with us. Marshal Hindenburg's name has become a symbol of the indestructible and forever vigorous spirit of the German people. The name of the President is inseparable from the name of the late Marshal. The greatest battle in historical boundaries is linked to the name of the late President Hindenburg and is inseparable. He served as the commander of the German army and saved the country from destruction. If our political leaders at that time had talents comparable to those of Hindenburg, then Germany could have avoided the deepest shame in history." Before Hitler spoke, a hundred musicians played Beethoven's Coriolanus Overture, which was broadcast by wireless radio to various parts of Germany and Italy, the United States, Japan, and other countries. After Hitler's speech, the band played a dirge again. After the meeting was dismissed, soldiers of the National Defense Army, the Black Shirt Guard of the National Socialist Party, the Guard of the Prussian Prime Minister General Goering, and the police all wore steel helmets and carried rifles with bayonets, and marched in formation through the Kroll Theater, saluting President Hitler, General Goering, and General von Blomberg. The deposed Crown Prince, wearing a military uniform, walked proudly, smiling to the crowd and left the hospital after shaking hands with the police, workers, and a girl in the crowd. He finally got into a blue sports car with a smile and drove away.

Today, the Kroll Theater was hung with black curtains and holly wreaths, decorated with white lotuses. Opposite the podium was a huge half-length statue of the late President, surrounded by flowers. Today, the authorities were extremely vigilant and had roped off the lamp posts to prevent the public from approaching the venue. Special wooden railings were also set up. On the road from the Prime Minister's Office to the Kroll Theater, armed guards stood shoulder to shoulder. Members of the National Socialist Party's Black Shirt Team held pistols and daggers, and mounted patrols held blades to prevent accidents. When President Hitler was about to leave the Prime Minister's Office to go to the Kroll Theater, there were two rows of police, standing on the left and right sides, and regarding the pure diplomatic issues of the Ambassador Plenipotentiary, his command and supervision, although still maintained as before, the command and supervision of general matters are governed by the Prime Minister. The ministers of various provinces participate in it. (2) A large organization composed of officials from the military and civilian ministries is newly established in the cabinet as an auxiliary agency for the Prime Minister on the Manchukuo issue. Also, the Army Ministry's plan for the Colonial Affairs Ministry is that it is too colonial and hinders the independence of Manchukuo. The Foreign Ministry's plan is considered to treat Manchukuo the same as a general independent country, which is also unacceptable, so it expressed opposition to both. (6th Dentsu News Agency)

Facing the crowd, several detachments of the National Defense Army were stationed at the Kroll Theater to guard it closely. The public was not allowed to walk within 200 yards of the theater, and even Hitler's followers were under close surveillance.

President Hitler carefully wrote his speech in the Prime Minister's Office last week, which he gave today and will give tomorrow at the funeral of the late President in Tannenberg. (6th Reuters)

Sweden's Neutral Policy

According to communist sources in the Swedish capital, German Defense Minister Blomberg recently visited the Swedish capital for a private tour and held secret talks with the Swedish government. Swedish Defense Minister Per Albin Hansson recently gave a speech clarifying that this statement is inaccurate, stating that General Blomberg did not go to the Swedish Ministry of Defense, nor did he meet with the Defense Minister. The Defense Minister has never considered inviting Blomberg to visit Sweden's defense arrangements. This matter must be clarified because the Swedish government's defense policy is solely for safeguarding peace and has no other purpose. This is the case now, and it will continue to be so in the future. As for forming alliances with other countries, this is not permitted within the scope of this policy, including forming alliances with countries along the Baltic Sea. The Social Democratic government does not want to hear about the policy of rearmament, but neither does it want a democratic Sweden to eliminate its strong defense tradition and the possibility of freedom. (Fifth Havas Dispatch)

Italian Naval Maneuvers

Mussolini Personally Observes the Maneuvers

The Italian First and Second Fleets began maneuvers today off the port of Gaeta, Italy. Prime Minister Mussolini arrived by seaplane to observe. The First Fleet is composed of several 10,000-ton cruisers, led by the "Zara." The Second Fleet has only several 5,000-ton cruisers. Each ship's average speed is above 25 knots. The exercise involves bombardment, with the target being a reef in the Gulf of Gaeta called Boot Rock. It is expected that by the time the exercise concludes tonight, it will have been destroyed and no longer appear on nautical charts. (Sixth Havas Dispatch)

Britain Stops Selling Cotton to Germany

(London) At the end of the week, cotton yarn exporters met in Manchester and decided that they would no longer ship cotton yarn to Germany until Germany pays off its debts and agrees on a method for paying for new goods. This move will greatly affect trade between Lancashire and Germany, and it is feared that 50,000 workers will lose their jobs directly or indirectly as a result. A British delegation is currently in Germany, and it is hoped that the delegation will resolve the issues as soon as possible. Exporters have extended the meeting to August 10. (Fifth Reuters Dispatch)

Soviet Russia Deceives Travelers

Riga Russian modern novelist and poet Ilya Ehrenburg recently formally stated to the Moscow authorities that the Russian travel agency provides foreign tourists visiting Russia with false and insincere hospitality, placing them in specially designated hotels and serving them with trained waiters, putting them in an atmosphere of prosperity and splendor. The purpose is to make tourists take away a good impression of the living conditions in Soviet Russia. The hotels have abundant food and drink, music, and dancing, with everything provided. As for the hunger, cold, and suffering of the people, which are the common experiences of the majority of people in Russia, they fear that foreign guests will see it. In fact, the good aspects of Soviet Russia should indeed be shown to people, but the bad aspects, such as the lack of food, the emptiness of the stores, the ragged clothing of the people, and the cruelty of people towards each other, cannot be concealed. Ehrenburg's writings are most famous in Germany, and his poems and essays have been translated into German. His writing is profound and sharp, and he is said to be a master of short essays. (Sixth Reuters Dispatch)

Soviet Collective Livestock Farms

(Moscow TASS News Agency, July 3) Since their collectivization at the same time as collective farms, Soviet livestock farms have occupied an important position in Soviet livestock husbandry. In total, there are 132,000 districts. The number of water buffalo raised in these districts was 5,400,000 in 1931, increasing to 6,400,000 this year. The number of pigs raised has increased from 2,100,000 in 1932 to 2,900,000 this year. Other livestock, such as flocks of sheep, have almost increased fivefold in the past two years. Collective livestock farms supply large numbers of livestock to collective farmers. In 1933, they obtained 170,000 calves (no fewer than 1,500,000 this year), 860,000 pigs (no fewer than 300,000 this year), and 100,000 lambs (no fewer than 500,000 this year). The Soviet Union is currently engaged in organizational work to improve livestock husbandry. Collective farms now have 1,935,000 calves, 45,000 piglets, and 125,000 sheep, and this year will continue to increase. Collective farms have made pioneering contributions to improving livestock conditions, establishing new-style pastures, and applying scientific methods. This year, the Soviet Union will also construct new-style pastures at a cost of over 400 million rubles.

Roosevelt's Speech

Harmonizing Agriculture and Industry in the East and West

Preserving the Sources of Agricultural and Industrial Profit

Preventing Manipulation by Individual Selfishness

(New York) President Roosevelt today broadcast a speech from Glacier National Park in Montana, stating that the government is now beginning to fight to preserve the sources of agricultural and industrial profit and to prevent manipulation by individual selfishness. He also stated that the East and West are closely related to each other, and the country must be regarded as a whole entity, not a collection of disjointed parts. This was the first public statement made by President Roosevelt after his tiring tour. (Fifth Reuters Dispatch)

Glacier National Park President Roosevelt delivered a radio address here today, and millions of people simultaneously heard the President explain his all-encompassing public works plan. This important speech was the President's first since his tour of Hawaii a month ago. His words were: "Our specific purpose is to build human happiness, which is also our way of making people more aware of the needs of the country. Today's people are no longer what they used to be and are all able to understand public welfare undertakings such as developing electricity, improving waterways, preventing floods and droughts, preventing forest fires, and balancing agriculture and industry. The government intends to develop industry in the West. In the past, the West overly emphasized agriculture and considered it sufficient to purchase industrial products from the East. The East has never paid much attention to agriculture. I know that the East and West are interdependent, but the country must think of the whole and not be regarded as a pile of loose sand." (Fifth National Dispatch)

(Washington) Since Roosevelt took office as President last March, he has been engaged in reversing the misfortune of the economic panic. Statistics released today by the Federal Reserve and the Department of Commerce are sufficient to prove that the President's efforts have made significant progress. The number of unemployed workers who have returned to work from the last month of Hoover's presidency to today has increased by 35%. Since the implementation of the New Deal, foreign trade has increased by 55%, and prices have increased by 23% due to the devaluation of the dollar and the restriction of agricultural production. The gradual recovery of industry and commerce can also be seen in the income of the railways. The income of the railways has increased by 31% compared to March 1933. The construction industry has increased by 85%, department store business has increased by 26%, and public confidence in national banks has been restored, which can be confirmed by the officially announced bank deposits. Since President Roosevelt ordered all banks to close a year ago and only allowed a few banks with excellent credit to reopen, bank deposits have increased by 25% to this day. (Fifth National Dispatch)

International Commercial Telegram

August 6th Reuters Special Business Report

Gold and Silver

London's Large Bars: The gold, silver, and large bar silver markets here are closed today, with no reports. New York Silver Futures: The distant month silver market opened here today, with prices shrinking from 10 pence to 70 pence compared to the closing price on Friday.

Bombay Large Bars: The Bombay silver market is stable today. The spot price is 58 rupees 6 annas, the August price is 58 rupees 7 annas, and the September price is 58 rupees 9 annas, all up by 3 annas.

Exchange Rates

New York Foreign Exchange Market: The market remains quiet today. The US-British exchange rate opened down 1.25 to $5.0425, then fell another 1.25 to $5.04125. This price has not changed before noon.

Securities

Before the opening of the New York securities market, the factors favorable to the market situation are: (1) activity in the steel industry area, now estimated to be about 37% of normal capacity, two points higher than before; (2) it is reported that London brokers are now advising people to buy American securities. The factors unfavorable to the market situation are: (1) merchants seem to be more pessimistic; (2) the future outlook remains uncertain. When the securities market opened, selling pressure broke out, and railway stocks were under pressure again. The securities market situation has a tendency to continue to decline because trading is very low.

Cotton and Wheat

US Cotton: The cotton market opened quietly, initially rising slightly, but later fell. The recent price for October futures is down 6 pence compared to the opening.

Indian Cotton: The Bombay cotton market initially rose due to speculation by speculators, but later softened due to selling by retail investors. The closing price for the April-May White Lohit cotton was 228.5 rupees, up 2 rupees.

US Wheat: The wheat market has not changed much, but there is also a downward trend in prices.

Rubber

New York opened up 7 pence, but the price soon fell. By 10:40 a.m., it had fallen by 6 pence.

The Panchen Lama Will Soon Leave Beiping

To Preach Sutras in Inner Mongolia in Mid-September

(Beiping) After the Panchen Lama arrived in Beiping from Nanjing, it was originally planned to stay in Beiping for a few days and then go to the residence of Prince Alashan in Inner Mongolia to escape the summer heat. However, due to the floods on the Ping-Sui Railway and the interruption of transportation, the departure date was postponed. According to a senior official in the Panchen Lama's entourage, the Panchen Lama has decided to leave Beiping for Inner Mongolia in the near future now that traffic on the Ping-Sui Railway has resumed. The Prince of Alashan arrived in Beiping earlier, urging him to leave quickly, and scheduled a sermon there in mid-September. It is reported that the Panchen Lama is scheduled to depart after the 14th of this month and has notified the Railway Bureau to prepare vehicles. General Fu Zuoyi telegraphed the Panchen Lama yesterday to welcome him and offered to prepare the Suiyuan Hotel as his residence. The Panchen Lama plans to stay in Suiyuan for a week. After that, he will go to Inner Mongolia. It is planned that the reincarnation of the Living Buddha Xing Sa of Qinghai will go north within days, first to Qinghai, to arrange everything. (Sixth Special Dispatch)

Wang Zhengting Arrived in Qingdao Yesterday

(Qingdao) Wang Zhengting arrived in Qingdao at 7:30 a.m. on the 6th from Jinan. After getting off the train, he attended the Jiaoji Railway Memorial Week and explained the significance of the New Life Movement in detail. He is scheduled to attend the Jiaoji Railway Board meeting on the 8th. Wang talked about the road redemption issue and hoped that the government would determine the policy to proceed with the purchase of the light railway. Matters related to the acquisition of light railways are not within the scope of the Board. Han Fuju paid his respects to Shen Ge and the officials stationed in Qingdao on the morning of the 6th, attended a banquet hosted by the five members of the Jiaoji Railway at noon, and went swimming in the sea in the evening. (Sixth Special Dispatch)

Gather in County Town to Request Relief

Anhui Security Team Goes to Suppress

(Anqing) According to a telegram from Wang Weicheng, the county magistrate of Wangjiang County, to the Provincial Government, the drought in the county is extremely severe, and ignorant farmers are gathering in the county town to request relief. The Provincial Government ordered Cai Bingyan, the director of the Security Department, to lead the First Battalion of the First Regiment of the Security Team at 9 p.m. on the 5th, taking the Anfeng and Anping patrol boats to suppress them. (Sixth Special Dispatch)

Hubei Disaster Relief and Famine Preparedness Committee

Held Its Inaugural Meeting at the Provincial Government

(Hankou) The Disaster Relief and Famine Preparedness Committee held its inaugural meeting at the Provincial Government today, chaired by Zhang Qun. He Hengfu, Meng Guangpeng, Li Fanyi, Ma Boyuan, and Zhou Zengtang were elected as standing committee members. The first meeting is scheduled for the 7th to discuss fundamental disaster relief measures and to urge all committee members to gather in the province to intensify their work. (Sixth Special Dispatch)

(Hankou) Li Jianai telegraphed that after the Xiangyang floods, there were heavy rains for two days, and the 49th District has become a swamp. The water is more than five feet deep, and refugees are flocking to the mountains to wait for rescue. Also, the severe drought in various counties has caused cries of despair. The Finance Department has specially borrowed 50,000 yuan from the Agricultural Bank of the Four Provinces to provide relief to rural areas and has detailed nine measures for reducing and exempting land taxes to correct the malpractices of clerks collecting taxes privately. (Sixth Special Dispatch)

(Hankou) Tai Bin telegraphed the province on the 6th, requesting that a work relief plan be drafted quickly and implemented through a meeting of the Finance Department and the National Economic Commission. (Sixth Special Dispatch)

The Yellow River's Water Level Rises Sharply

(Jinan) The Yellow River within the province is rising sharply. At Lishan Tun upstream, it rose 2.4 inches, at Luokou in the midstream, it rose 4.8 inches, and at Xiezhi Bay downstream, it rose 2.3 inches. On the 4th, the Dengquan River in Yucheng breached its banks, and the water flowed northeast, entering the Tuhai River through the territory of the Jihe River. It is more than 20 miles long and 2-3 to 8-9 miles wide. Countless fields, houses, and autumn crops were submerged. (Sixth Special Dispatch)

(Tianjin) The Yellow River in southern Hebei has risen by one meter, and the beaches on both banks have been flooded. The water has submerged the Sixth Embankment. After inspection and blocking by the Post-Disaster Relief Engineering Office, there was no danger. Today, the Post-Disaster Relief Engineering Office telegraphed the province for emergency assistance. (Sixth Special Dispatch)

Drought Almost Throughout Jiangxi

(Nanchang) The drought has spread almost throughout the province, and even miscellaneous grains cannot be replanted. The price of late rice in this city has risen by 7-8 jiao per day. It is currently 12 yuan per dan, and there is no market. The authorities will stop issuing rice transport permits and will have the financial community invest in transporting rice to the province. The Economic Commission has decided to spend 200,000 to build the Quan Gang sluice gates in Qingjiang, Gaoan, and Fengcheng counties to irrigate the fields. The headquarters has allocated 200,000 from the Agricultural Bank of the Four Provinces to purchase more than ten pumping machines, which have been distributed to various counties. (Sixth Special Dispatch)

Chiang Instructs Jiangsu and Zhejiang Provinces

To Properly Draft Disaster Prevention Plans

Chiang Kai-shek of Guling recently telegraphed the chairmen of the provincial governments of Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Jiangxi, Henan, Hubei, and Anhui, saying: "The way to provide disaster relief depends on early prevention at ordinary times and well-thought-out remediation in emergencies. Therefore, in ancient times, three years of cultivation were sure to have one year's worth of food. And in recent years, I have repeatedly ordered the provinces to prepare grain storage and urged the provinces to promote rural cooperation, etc. The meaning is in this. Since this year, floods and droughts have occurred repeatedly, and the disaster area is wide, extending to several provinces. To find out the reason, it is really because the provincial authorities lack defensive measures, so that when there is a drought, there is no irrigation, and when there is a flood, there is no way to divert it. They sit and watch the disaster become a reality, and they only know how to panic and shout. When they review their duties, do they have no guilt? It is like the situation in the provinces along the Yangtze River since the summer of this year. There has been little rainfall, and the fields are dry. Although this is a disaster, if you study carefully and adapt to local conditions, it is not difficult to draw water to relieve the emergency in areas where rivers and streams crisscross. In high-lying areas near mountains, it is also advisable to plan for drought-resistant crops to improve the situation. At the same time, we should make great efforts in adjusting rural food supplies, financial relief, and all matters related to disaster prevention. We may not have exhausted our means. However, the provincial authorities have not heard of putting their heart and soul into this, but they only use broad and general words to report disasters and famine, or even exaggerate the reports in the newspapers, hoping to make a sensation and prepare the way to request funds and raise relief funds. As for the actual situation, whether the disaster situation in their area is really as reported, how much damage has been suffered, and whether it has reached a point where there is nothing that can be done and it cannot be salvaged, I am afraid that even the disaster-reporting officials may not fully understand the details. In this situation, it is only possible to make preparations and is only a laughingstock of society. Speaking of this, I am really moved. Now, for the sake of thinking about troubles and preventing them, learning from the past and preventing future occurrences, all disaster prevention plans for the coming year in your province should be carefully designed by the provincial government according to what it can do, and specific measures and budget estimates should be drafted in detail. Those that should be carried out but cannot be borne by the province's human and financial resources, and those that require a longer period of time to complete, should also be drafted in a three-year or five-year plan, with a budget determined, and submitted to this headquarters before October 1 of this year for verification. In addition, public agricultural fields and cooperative undertakings that are beneficial to disaster prevention should be promoted and appropriately rewarded, and the Kangji Record, which was re-printed and distributed by this headquarters last year, contains many methods for preventing and relieving disasters and curing the root and the symptoms of the disease throughout the generations, which are sufficient for today's reference and borrowing. It can also be studied in detail and adopted with reference to the actual situation. It is necessary to ensure that disaster prevention facilities, the government guides from above, and the people work hard from below, so that the effect is more significant, and there will be no worries about digging a well when you are thirsty. In the future, when the provinces report disasters, they must also wait for a thorough investigation to confirm the situation and the estimated amount of crop failure, and report the details truthfully. Do not exaggerate or lie, and do not issue public documents or publish them in the newspapers, so as to avoid being impractical. In addition to separate telegrams and other orders, all must be complied with as required." (Sixth Central News Agency Dispatch)

Unprecedented Drought in Zhejiang Province

Suicides Are Rumored Everywhere

(Hangzhou) The unprecedented drought in Zhejiang Province has become hopeless. Suicides are rumored everywhere. Recently, a visitor from Pujiang County said that in Jiangwu Tang, a place in the eastern countryside of the county, eleven members of a family, old and young, male and female, all committed suicide by taking arsenic, and only a twelve-year-old grandson survived because he refused to take poison. It is also said that a family of eight in a certain village also committed suicide. It was a terrible tragedy. (Sixth Central News Agency Dispatch)

Ma Heng Granted One Month's Leave

(Nanjing) According to the Executive Yuan, Ma Heng, the director of the Palace Museum, who is in Beiping for domestic affairs, telegraphed the Executive Yuan to request one month's leave. The Executive Yuan granted the leave, and the duties of the museum are to be handled by a proxy. (Sixth Special Dispatch)

Military Headquarters Orders Military Hospitals

To Impose Restrictions on Patients with Minor Illnesses

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Military Affairs forwarded the instructions of the Military Medical Department. Recently, it has been found that many military hospitals admit patients with minor illnesses from various units at their own request. At this time of year, when the hospitals are crowded in the summer, how can patients with minor illnesses be allowed to occupy beds? From now on, patients with minor illnesses will still be treated by the units themselves, and hospital beds must not be occupied. On the 6th, orders were sent to the directors of all hospitals to implement this strictly. All patients admitted to the hospital must be carefully inspected, and those who have recovered must be discharged at any time to facilitate new admissions. (Sixth Special Dispatch)

Military Commission

Promulgates an Outline of Personnel Affairs

(Nanjing) The Military Commission stated that in recent years, personnel matters in various agencies and units have often been based on expediency and have not been handled in accordance with regulations, resulting in frequent changes and no basis for evaluation. If this continues, not only will there be constant transfers, making it difficult to settle down, but it will also encourage the desire for advancement, which will have a huge impact on the future of the national army. It is essential to add restrictions and determine guarantees to correct this. Now that the bandit threat is gradually subsiding, the reorganization of personnel is even more urgent. The personnel regulations promulgated in the past are not yet complete. The Personnel Evaluation Department of the Commission convened meetings of various related agencies to amend them separately. From now on, military officers must first be appointed in accordance with laws and regulations before being assigned to positions. Yesterday, the "Implementation Procedures for Military Officers of the Army, Navy, and Air Force" and the "Outline of Personnel Affairs for Military Officers of the Army, Navy, and Air Force" were distributed to all subordinate agencies and units for strict compliance. (Sixth Special Dispatch)

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Interior re-consulted the provinces and cities to ban the banknotes of the Republic of China Bank in order to prevent the villagers from being deceived. (Sixth Special Dispatch)

Disaster Area in Hubei Province Expands

Disaster Victims Snatch Food, Flee, and Commit Suicide

Ten Gentlemen Request 5 Million Yuan for Disaster Relief

Hankou Correspondence. After the major flood in Hubei Province, it was followed by severe drought. The disaster-stricken area has already reached forty counties, and the number of affected people is no less than ten million. To this day, it has not rained for many days, causing the disaster area to expand day by day, and the number of disaster victims to increase. Robbing food, fleeing, and committing suicide are happening everywhere. The problem is serious, even more so than the flood in the twentieth year of the Republic. In addition to resolutely stopping the construction of new government offices and transferring 500,000 yuan of construction funds to provide relief, the provincial government has repeatedly appealed to all parties, at least to raise 2 million yuan for relief funds, so that emergency relief, work relief, and agricultural relief can be carried out in sequence. On the 4th, the Provincial Relief Committee convened a meeting of gentry from all over the province, raising four questions: (1) How to determine the method of raising relief funds; (2) How to raise relief funds; (3) How to distribute relief funds after raising them; (4) What kind of seeds should be tested so that they are suitable for the land in each county and can be replanted. The opinions of the gentry can be summarized into seven points: (1) Determine the amount of disaster relief to be 5 million yuan; (2) Issue disaster relief bonds and disaster relief lottery tickets; (3) Expand disaster relief publicity and issue disaster relief reward and punishment regulations; (4) Use the 370,000 yuan of savings under the Sino-Foreign Famine Relief Fund for emergency relief; (5) Request the Rural Financial Relief Office of the Four Provinces Farmers Bank to find ways to provide relief to rural areas in various counties; (6) Open up stockpiled grain; (7) Exempt the mu tax. Except for necessary donations, all other donations and taxes will be suspended. Meng Guangpeng, chairman of the Relief Association, expressed his acceptance of all of these. In the past, the collection of field taxes in various counties was quite strict. Now, due to the severity of the disaster and the difficulties of the people, a special change has been made to the original plan, and six separate methods have been formulated in accordance with the disaster relief regulations issued by the Ministry and the customs of the province: (1) Those affected by more than 90% of the disaster will be exempted from 80% of the regular tax; (2) Those affected by 80% of the disaster will be exempted from 60% of the regular tax; (3) Those affected by 70% of the disaster will be exempted from 50% of the regular tax; (4) Those affected by 60% of the disaster will be exempted from 30% of the regular tax; (5) Those affected by 50% of the disaster will be exempted from 20% of the regular tax; (6) For those with more serious crop failures that are close to becoming a disaster, 10% of the regular tax will be exempted. The benefits to the disaster victims are by no means small. However, it is still unknown whether the mu tax, which is related to security, can be reduced. (5th)

Severe Drought in Jiangxi Becomes More Serious

The Number of Counties Reporting Disasters Has Exceeded Half

Rice Prices Soar and Everything is Expensive

Nanchang Correspondence. Since the heavy rain on June 15th and 16th in this province, the weather has been scorching hot and not a drop of rain has fallen. On June 27th, Little Heat, the paddy fields in slightly higher terrain and farther from water have already experienced drought. Since Little Heat, the drought has been extremely severe, the fields have cracked, and the color of the rice has turned yellow. In previous years, 70% to 80% of the early rice would have matured by Little Heat, but this year, due to the excessively cold weather in April, most of the early rice has rotted and the rice seedlings were planted too late, resulting in slow development. Although Little Heat has arrived, they have not been able to bear fruit. At the same time, many of the late rice seedlings have also withered and turned yellow. Two-season rice must be sown after the early rice is harvested. Now, there is no water for planting rice seedlings anywhere, so there is no hope at all. The farmers are trying their best to scoop water to save the fields near the water, but the higher fields are cracked with gaps as wide as several inches. The rice seedlings are as red as the needles of withered pine trees, as if they were on fire and about to burn. At present, out of the 81 counties and 5 special administrative districts in this province, 41 counties and districts, including Linchuan, Shangrao, Shanggao, Wuning, and Yangxi, have reported drought. The disaster situation in the counties in the bandit areas is even more tragic. The head of Suichuan County telegraphed the relief committee, saying that the residents of Wudoujiang and other places are struggling to survive on grass roots and tree bark under the double disaster of banditry and drought. If Suichuan is like this, then the situations in Yu, Rui, Hui, Xing, Shi, and other bandit areas can be imagined.

In this city, rice prices have soared in the past ten days, from 6 yuan to 10.05 yuan, and are still continuing to rise. The prices of all other goods have also risen accordingly. Vegetables are twice as expensive as in May and June. In the past, 1 yuan could buy 7.5 jin of oil, but now it can only buy 6 jin. The general public feels that the drought is becoming more serious due to the rising prices. As for relief, the provincial government has approved the Executive Headquarters to allocate 200,000 yuan from the Four Provinces Farmers Bank to purchase water-lifting machines. It is said that more than ten seats have been ordered and will be transported soon. There are no specific measures for drilling wells and diverting water, which require too much expense and will not help in time. If it can rain before the Beginning of Autumn, the farmers will replant buckwheat, beans, and other miscellaneous grains in the hope of compensating for the loss. (2nd)

Internal Disintegration of Xiao's Bandits

| Bandit Leader Disguises Himself as a Soldier to Avoid Assassination |

Nanchang Correspondence. The Jiangxi Executive Headquarters reported, according to the report from the head of Taihe County, that seven bandits with guns surrendered to the Bao Lian Office in Qiaotou on the 26th, and they reported that there were five companies of bandits stationed in Qiaotou, with more than 500 guns, and three companies stationed in Jindong, with more than 300 guns. The bandits, realizing that they were in a desperate situation, and because they had recently been bombed by planes and feared destruction, were surrendering one after another. Half of the bandits in Qiaotou have fled, and more than one company of troops has also left Jindong. Most of them detoured back to Yongcheng, and hundreds of them have also surrendered to the eighth district of the county and the seventh district of Ji'an. It was found that most of the squad leaders and above in the bandit unit were from Hunan, and most of the soldiers were from Yongxin. Recently, the oppression by the officers has reached its extreme. Not only have they lost their fighting ability, but they all intend to surrender with their guns. The bandit leader Xiao Ke and other important officers have all disguised themselves as soldiers, partly to prevent soldiers from rioting and being assassinated, and partly to pretend to be soldiers and surrender in desperation. According to the above information, the bandit army has indeed disintegrated internally. Now, we are using both suppression and pacification, and it can be expected that the remaining bandits in western Jiangxi will be wiped out soon.

Also, a report from Xu Yuanquan said that the bandits entrenched in the mountainous area bordering Lichuan and Xianfeng counties include Wang Wencheng, Hua Shuntao, and Liu Han. After repeated dispatches of troops to suppress them, they fled back to the Bajiatai, Xiaodongping, and Huodongping areas in Xian County. It was recently heard that Wang, under the pretext of summoning Hua and Liu to a meeting at the Qianyanjiaodong Cave, had already taken revenge on Hua and Liu and killed Wang Wencheng. Wang's younger brother led the remaining bandits to flee to the northwest of Dachun. It has been ordered to the various units to pursue and suppress the bandits in different directions in order to completely eliminate them. (August 5th)

Critical Situation on the Grand Canal in Liaocheng

| The Construction Department Orders Qingping and Linqing Counties to Remove Earth Dams |

Jinan Correspondence. Due to heavy rains and the influx of water, the water level in the Grand Canal in Liaocheng, Shandong Province, has risen sharply. The downstream is blocked by earth dams, and the discharge is slow, causing dangerous conditions. The Construction Department received a telegram from Sun Tongfeng, the magistrate of the county, yesterday, saying that the water in the Grand Canal was turbulent. Because it was blocked by earth dams between Qingping and Linqing, it could not flow downstream, causing the embankment behind the Iron Pagoda Temple outside the North Gate to almost collapse. Fortunately, the people desperately rushed to block it, and it was able to turn the corner. According to the telegram, the Construction Department urgently telegraphed Qingping and Linqing counties yesterday (the 4th) to quickly remove the earth dams in order to discharge the accumulated water from the upper reaches. At the same time, it replied to Liaocheng for information. Also, Sun Tongfeng, the magistrate of Liaocheng County, telegraphed the provincial government of Han Fuqu, reporting the latest situation of the Grand Canal and asking him to quickly order Qingping and Linqing counties to open the gates to release water. Han asked the Construction Department for information. The telegram read, "I recently received a telephone call from Sun Tongfeng, the magistrate of Liaocheng County, reporting that the water level in the Grand Canal in this county has risen sharply. All dangerous situations of bridges and embankments outside the North Gate being washed away have been reported in telegrams. Now, I will report the latest situation again. 1. The water in the Grand Canal continues to rise, originating from the water from Yanggu Taochengpu and the Twelve Lianwa, which flows northward. 2. The water level in the Grand Canal in Qingping and Linqing counties is not high. Please telegraph the two counties to open the gates to release water in order to discharge the water. 3. The embankment at the intersection of the Grand Canal and the Tuhai River has collapsed, leaving only one meter of width. We are currently leading laborers to reinforce it. 4. The embankments on the east and west banks of the Grand Canal behind the Great Temple in the East Gate of this city are very thin and are in danger. We are still supervising the group police and laborers to do their best to protect them. 5. Water seepage on the west bank of the intersection of the Grand Canal and the Zhou Gong River is being prevented. In addition to sending a separate telegram to the head of the Construction Department, I hereby telegraph this report. Why are the Qingping and Linqing counties not opening the gates? Please investigate the reason and report it for verification and decision. (Signed) Chairman Han Fuqu." After receiving the telegram, the Construction Department immediately replied, "In response to your secret telegram, reporting the situation of the Grand Canal rising sharply according to the telephone report from the magistrate of Liaocheng County, and requesting that Qingping and Linqing counties be telegraphed to open the gates to release water, and ordering the reason why the two counties did not open the gates to be presented for verification and decision, it was found that there were no gates built in the Qingping and Linqing counties. The old abandoned gates also have no gates, so there should be no water obstruction. The reason for the water rise in Liaocheng is that the river crossing roads in Liangshui Town, Qingping County Weiwan, Daiwan, 20-li Pu, and the second gate behind the Jinde Society in the west gate of Linqing County 20-li Pu are all earth dams, and there are no bridge holes for water discharge. When the river was dredged, the Dredging and Treatment of the Grand Canal Project Office of this department was afraid of obstructing traffic and temporarily reserved them, and ordered them to be removed during the flood season. Recently, according to the separate telegram from Liaocheng County to the department, strict telegrams have been sent to the counties in the lower reaches, ordering them to quickly mobilize laborers to excavate all the earth dams that block water to facilitate discharge, and the handling situation has been sent by letter to the secretariat of your office for submission. Now, in response to the previous cause, the Construction Department, Zhang Honglie, bows and reports for your inspection." (5th)

Songjiang County Government Urges Opium Smokers to Register

The county government of this county previously received an order from the province to form a committee to handle opium suppression matters. It has issued a notice to the various sub-stations and rural townships to inform opium smokers to register. However, opium smokers are watching each other, so since the registration began on June 1st, few have registered in the past two months. Now, County Chief Jin has issued a proclamation, stating that the deadline for opium smokers to apply for registration was originally from June 1st to August 31st, which is the registration period for opium smokers. Now, it has been found that two-thirds of the deadline has passed. Opium smokers under your jurisdiction are urged to go to the local public security office to apply for registration. If they fail to report after the deadline, not only will they no longer be issued licenses, but once they are discovered or reported, they will be treated as opium offenders and reported to the provincial government and forwarded to the Military Commission for handling in accordance with military law. Do not wait and see and delay yourselves. Now that the deadline is approaching, more opium smokers are gradually registering.

Prolonged Drought, No Rain, and Cracked Rice Fields

The weather has been hot recently, and the temperature indoors often exceeds 100 degrees. There has been no rain for almost a month. The river water has dried up, and the riverbed is completely exposed during the day. Residents have difficulty with drinking water and irrigating farmland. Wuxi Farmers Block Chengxi Automobiles

The waterway between Xicheng Province and the fourth bridge near Sitou Town, due to drought and dry water, the bottom of the bridge is more than three feet higher than the bottom of the river, and the water flow is blocked, resulting in more than 6,000 mu of farmland north of the bridge that rely on irrigation being dry. The crowd clamored and reported to the Construction Bureau, which invited Sun Chenchu of the Xicheng Long-distance Automobile Company to negotiate. It was agreed that the Construction Bureau would cooperate with the district township head to allocate a water-lifting machine to be stationed at the Luoxia Bridge next to the fourth bridge day and night for rescue. The Xicheng Automobile Company posted 200 yuan for the diesel engine worker's salary, paying 100 yuan first and the remaining 100 yuan to be paid on August 4th. Now that the due date has arrived, the villagers specially sent Hua Wenjie to the company to collect it. However, the company claimed that it had not been paid. The villagers, believing that the company had broken its promise, immediately gathered six or seven hundred people, each carrying hoes and iron rakes, and waited in full force on the bridge deck, preparing to dismantle the bridge, resulting in traffic being blocked. A total of seven large cars and nine small cars were blocked. After five or six hours, a major disaster almost occurred. Fortunately, District Chief Jiang Zhizhong arrived to mediate and promised to pay the money, and then everyone dispersed and traffic resumed.

Rice Prices Skyrocket to 12 Yuan

The rice market has been rising wildly in recent days, and the trend is becoming stronger and stronger. The reason is that rice prices in various places such as Beijing, Shanghai, Wuhu, and Tianjin have also been rising recently, so purchasing agents are very interested. After the rice market opened yesterday, japonica and indica grains all rose by 4 or 5 jiao. White japonica rice has reached the 12 yuan mark, followed by 11.4 yuan, machine white 13 yuan to 12.5 yuan, machine big indica 10.09 yuan to 10.04 yuan, machine guest indica 9.55 yuan to 8.8 yuan, coarse japonica rice 10.06 yuan to 10 yuan, japonica paddy 5.65 yuan to 5.5 yuan, yuan paddy 6.5 yuan to 6.35 yuan, big indica paddy 5.15 yuan to 5 yuan, guest indica paddy 4.55 yuan to 4.2 yuan, Du wheat 6.12 yuan to 6.1 yuan.

Model Area Promotes Silkworm Rearing Guidance

In order to promote the scope of silkworm rearing guidance and improve the effectiveness of guidance, the office of the Silkworm and Mulberry Model Area of this county, in accordance with the regulations of the Jiangsu Provincial Silkworm Industry Improvement and Management Committee, has established five central guidance centers in the silkworm and mulberry centers of the county. The first central area is located in Banqiao Beizhuang, with instructors You Zhenhua, Yin Hong, and Zhang Qirong, covering the townships of Yangming, Xin'an, and Kaihua. The second central area is located in Houzhai, with instructors Wu Junmei, Gao Shu, and Chen Yige, covering the townships of Taibo and Nanyan. The third central area is located in Donghutang, with instructors Wang Shiyi, Gu Wanying, and Yin Shuzhen, covering the townships of Huai Shang, Huai Xia, and Bei Shang. The fourth central area is located in Xizhang, with instructors Xu Yiru and Chen Yi, covering the townships of Tianshang, Tianxia, and Qingcheng. The fifth central area is located in Outangqiao, with instructors Wu Mengying, Tan Zhiyun, and Xue Suojuan, covering the townships of Kaihua, Wan'an, Fu'an, and Kaiyuan. Each district is divided into several guidance sub-centers. A total of 88 sub-centers have been established in the county, with as many as 170 or 180 instructors. All of them have been hired to Xicheng and are scheduled to depart for the countryside around the 10th of this month to engage in autumn silkworm work.

Strange Pests Found in Mashan, Changzhou

The eleventh district of Wu County is located in the lake and is different from other districts. Recently, a kind of insect that damages crops has been discovered in the four villages of Taohua, Yong'an, Shenxian, and Zhaiquan near Majishan. The insects resemble white worms and specialize in gnawing rice seedlings. More than a dozen acres of fields have been damaged by them. The villagers felt that they had never seen this kind of pest before and found it very strange. They tried to catch them, but the insects all hid in the mud, making it impossible to exterminate them. As a result, panic arose and the insects are spreading daily, already reaching four villages. Ding Zhigui, the head of the district, reported that he went to inspect the situation himself and also felt powerless to eliminate them. So he captured several pests and brought them to the city on the 6th, and took them to the county government on the morning of the 7th to study them and ask for methods of extermination.

Shen Baixian and Others from Haimen Go to Hai for Inspection

Shen Baixian, the director of the Jiangsu Provincial Construction Department, Zhao Zhiyou, the chairman of the Yangtze River Waterway Management Committee, and Song Xishang, the director of the Engineering Department, arrived in Tongcheng yesterday (the 4th) on the Lijian ferry to plan the soil protection project in the county. Zhang Weixie, the magistrate of this county, Chen Guiqing, the magistrate of Jingjiang County, Wang Bin, the magistrate of Chongming County, and Li Baojian, the magistrate of Qidong County, who had finished attending the administrative conference in Tongcheng, accompanied Shen, Zhao, Song, and others to Hai today (the 5th) at 9:00 AM to inspect the Dasheng Third Factory and the Qinglonggang Waterway, and instructed the key points of the Puchi (Pukou to Qidong) Road project. At 12:00, people from all walks of life had a banquet at the County Chamber of Commerce, and in the afternoon, they took a special car to the reclamation area and then went to Rugao.

Yangtze River Downstream Treatment Project in Nantong

The current situation of the Yangtze River is deteriorating, especially the section from Jiangyin to Haikou. The river surface between Nantong and Changshu is 80 to 90 li wide, and the river is studded with silt and sand, which the shipping industry regards as a dangerous place. Since there is so much silt and sand, the river flow has changed direction, and the north bank has been severely eroded. Nantong has suffered the most. Zhao Zhiyou, the chairman of the Yangtze River Waterway Management Committee, Song Xishang, the director of the Engineering Department, and Shen Baixian, the director of the Jiangsu Provincial Construction Department, specially came to Tongcheng on the 4th and took the Lijian ferry in the morning and afternoon to survey the area along the river, and decided to carry out the downstream treatment, which will be implemented by the River Management Committee. The plan is to build two jetties at Haibeigang, 30 li upstream of the Langshan River in Nantong. Two stone jetties will be built in the Chanyin Sand Section and Shansha Section to the vicinity of Buyugang. Four jetties will be built between Yaogang and Rengang. This is the first step of the project. After implementation, more than 2,000 mu of sand can be raised outside Haibeigang to form fields, worth more than 2 million yuan. The second step of the project is to build 11 stone jetties in Changyin Sand. The total cost of the front and rear projects is 400,000 yuan. If all of them are completed, the river flow will definitely change direction, and the silt and sand in the Tongzhou River will definitely be washed into the sea by the rapid flow. Since the water flow is straight, it should not wash away the banks anymore. As for the current palliative treatment, Song, the director of the Engineering Department, specially instructed Zhou Kebao, the director of the Nantong Construction Bureau, to rush to repair the jetties on the river surface that have not yet sunk. On the one hand, the Waterway Association will send a survey team to Tongcheng to measure the water depth along the river. The River Management Committee will construct according to the survey.

Careless Incident at Funing Shen Gan's Kerosene Store

Shen Gan's store, located on the South Main Street of this city, which deals in foreign oil, rented tile-roofed houses behind the Catholic Church on East Street as a kerosene storage depot last year. Suddenly, at 2:30 PM yesterday, a fire broke out, and flames soared into the sky. The entire city was covered in smoke, obscuring the sun, and the smell of oil filled the air, creating a terrifying scene. Over a hundred households in the vicinity hired boats and hurriedly moved their belongings. Fortunately, the Provincial Security Team stationed here and various fire brigades rushed to the scene and desperately fought the fire, preventing it from spreading to nearby buildings. They also managed to salvage over two hundred boxes of foreign oil. It is estimated that over a thousand boxes of kerosene, along with hundreds of boxes each of matches and paper cigarettes, and over a hundred packages of foreign sugar, and over four hundred boxes of Sunlight soap, totaling over ten thousand dollars, were destroyed. The fire was finally extinguished at 6:30 PM. The cause of the fire remains unknown. Six firefighters were injured and have been sent to the hospital for treatment.

Bandits Occupy Yangji Town

It has been reported in this newspaper that the home of Liu Ruwei in Yangji Town, within the fourth district of this county, was robbed and murdered by bandits yesterday. It is now learned that the bandits have gathered over two hundred people and are occupying the vicinity of Qinggou, hiding during the day and venturing out at night. The local population is unable to resist. Whenever troops are dispatched, the bandits flee into the marshes, leaving no trace. As soon as the troops leave, they return with renewed force. Yesterday at midnight, the bandits once again occupied Yangji Town. It is reported that the Headquarters of the Defense Corps has devised a plan for a forceful suppression.

Tragic News of Suicides Among Flood Victims in Jiashan

The severe drought in this county continues, and the areas of Dayun, Zhanghui, and others have also been afflicted by rice borers, leading to a hopeless autumn harvest and a lack of sustenance. Frequent reports of peasants in the countryside hanging themselves or taking poison have been heard. We hereby report the facts: (1) Wang A'shi, a farmer from Huoshanjing, married to a woman named Wang, worked diligently in the fields. However, the river channels dried up, making irrigation impossible, and the young seedlings withered long ago. Wang's wife went out to help others draw water, but all her wages were taken by her aunt, who spent them all. When she asked her aunt for the money back, she was scolded. Overwhelmed by the hardship of life and the abuse, Wang's wife suddenly became suicidal and hanged herself on the night before last. (2) Shen A'quan, a farmer from Changbang in the Yong'an district, owned only seven mu of land, making it difficult to support his family. Adding to this, the severe drought withered the rice, making recovery impossible. Witnessing this, A'quan abandoned his wife and children and disappeared without a trace. His wife cried all day and, left with no other choice, took her young daughter and drowned in the river. (3) Shen Sanguan, a farmer from Zhonggangjing, and Zhang Siqing, a farmer from Fushanjing, both committed suicide due to starvation. Such tragic events are occurring incessantly, which is truly lamentable.

Bandits from Gaoyou Plunder Cargo Ships

The Tianhua Kerosene Company and Lishengheng General Merchandise Store in Linze Town of this county dispatched ships to Xinghua to transport goods the day before yesterday, carrying over seven hundred silver dollars. However, when they reached the Yangzilincao Marsh, they encountered six bandit ships with fifty to sixty bandits who had been routed by government troops from Xiaogezhuang. The bandits ordered them to stop, jumped onto the cargo ships, and conducted a thorough search. They not only stole all the money but also kidnapped Chen, the young clerk escorting the ships, and sailed eastward.

Bandits Zhu Zhongren and Others Executed by Firing Squad in Jingjiang

Jingjiang, located in the remote north of the Yangtze River, is a place with little land and a dense population. In recent years, due to rural bankruptcy, many undesirable elements have become bandits, leading to frequent robberies and causing considerable harm. Last month, the home of Gao Chengyuan in the eighth district was robbed by bandits, and the owner was injured. Subsequently, Captain Wang of the Security Department and Xuan Ming, the head of the county government's task force, rushed to the countryside at night and arrested the main culprits, Zhu Zhongren, Wang Jinzhang, Li Xiaogouzi, Wu Liuxiao, and others. After interrogation by Judge Bao Cheng, they confessed to their crimes. The case was immediately reported to the provincial government, which issued a telegram approving the death penalty. After receiving the telegram, the county government verified the identities of Zhu Zhongren and others, tied them to the execution ground, and executed them by firing squad.

Letter Received

Having read the report in the "Various County Communications" column on page three of your newspaper on July 27th, which stated that "Zhou Zhiqing, the water patrol chief of Lingdian Port in Haimen, was caught smoking opium in the home of a prostitute (Xiao Honglin) at 3 PM on the 22nd of this month. Over two hundred opium pills were seized, and he has been taken to the bureau for investigation," we find this very surprising. Lingdian Port is under the jurisdiction of our detachment, and there is no one named Zhou Zhiqing among the patrol chiefs or water patrols of our entire detachment. We fear the report is inaccurate, and we are writing to your newspaper to request a correction. Sincerely, Xu Guozhang, Captain of the First Detachment, Thirteenth Team, Third District, Jiangsu Provincial Maritime Public Security Force, to the Editorial Department of Shen Bao.
