Local News

French Navy in China

Conducted Large-Scale Maneuvers in Waters off Zhoushan Yesterday

French Warships from Shanghai Sailed to Participate in Maneuvers

French Consulate General Notified Zhejiang Provincial Government

The French Far East Naval Fleet, under the command of Rear Admiral Lax, has decided to hold large-scale maneuvers in Zhejiang waters. The waters off Zhoushan have been selected as the location for the French warships to conduct their exercises. The exercise dates have been set from the afternoon of the 6th of this month to the 16th, for a total of ten days.

French Warships Set Sail

Some French warships stationed in China remain docked in Shanghai, while others are on patrol. For these maneuvers, Rear Admiral Lax, the French naval commander, has summoned all ships to Zhoushan to participate. The cruisers Premengue and the gunboat S de Brazza, stationed in Shanghai, completed their preparations yesterday morning and set sail from Songkou to join the exercises. The dispatch vessel Savorgnan de Brazza and the flagship D’Entrecasteaux are also expected to sail to Zhoushan to participate.

Commander to Observe Maneuvers

Rear Admiral Lax, the commander of the French Far East Naval Fleet, has decided to personally observe the maneuvers to facilitate command. However, he will wait until the warships have conducted several days of preliminary exercises before boarding the flagship D’Entrecasteaux on the 11th of this month to travel to Zhoushan. The admiral also plans to stay in the Zhoushan Islands for a period of leisure after the exercises.

Notification to Zhejiang Province

The French Navy’s exercises are scheduled for ten days, during which all aspects of naval warfare will be practiced. Live ammunition will be used, and searchlights will be deployed at night, which differs from previous years. Therefore, the French Consul General in Shanghai, Mr. Meyrier, has notified the Zhejiang Provincial Government to inform residents along the coast of Zhoushan and to notify all commercial vessels, fishing boats, and civilian vessels traveling in Zhejiang waters to remain calm.

Bank Savings Association Trust Company

Held a Joint Tea Party Yesterday

Unanimous Agreement to Adhere to Principles of Bank Savings Law

But Requesting Modifications to Provisions of Law That Are Difficult to Implement

Following the promulgation of the Savings Bank Law, the Banking Association decided to request amendments. Yesterday afternoon at 4 PM, the association hosted a joint tea party at its clubhouse on Hong Kong Road, inviting banks, trust companies, and savings associations from across the city. A unanimous resolution was passed to request amendments to provisions of the law that are difficult to implement. Details are as follows:

Joint Tea Party

Yesterday's joint tea party was attended by Hu Gesheng of Hua An, Chen Ziai of Zhizhong, Zhang Cantang of Wuhua, Chen Guangqing of Guanghua, Shen Binzhang of Yadong, Zhu Qinpu of Zhengming, Lu Mengfu of China Industrial Development, Jin Caisheng of China Industrial, Chen Shizhen of Hong Kong National, Wu Weiru of Donglai, Yu Zhongyan of Huizhong, Xu Ruizhang of Siming Savings Association, Cai Songfu of Dunxu, Qi Yunqing of Nonggong, Tong Xianting of Zhonghua, Wei Shouren of Jiangzhe, Xu Boming of Jiangsu, Hu Xianshi of Siming, Shen Hegao of Jia Hua, Wang Chengzhi of Taiping, Yu Shouchun of Tongshang, Bao Chengde of Jianghai, Shi Boqun of Six Banks, Xu Rihkang of Xintong, Mi Xialing of Zhonghe, Huang Mohan of Juxingcheng, Gu Wensheng of Jiande, Chen Qinghua of Dalai, Chen Dairu of Zhejiang, Lin Pingfu of Guotai, Xia Gaoxiang of Qiye, Zhang Zhanglu of Guohua, Yuan Jiatang of Jiangnan, Zou Cuihua of Southeast Trust, Hua Shuochen of Tonghui Trust, Dong Huixun of Fu Dian, Wang Boyuan of Kenye, Chen Zisheng of Central Trust, Pei Huizhi of Women's, Xu Xuegeng of Xintai, Yao Yinpeng of Zhonghui, Zhang Zhuyu of Guohuo, Tang Shoumin of Jiaotong, Zhou Zongyun of Zhongnan, Shen Bingheng of Bianye, Chen Zheqing of Yan Ye, Miao Zhendong of Minghua, Shu Luzhong of Huifeng, Li Wenjie of Tongyi Trust, Chen Guangfu of Shanghai, Wu Zhihao of Ningbo, Xie Yuru of World, Yuan Mengling of Quangong, Ma Changsheng of Shanghai National, Wu Rongqing of Minfu, Le Gengrong of Hengli, Wang Zhixin of Xinhua, Ye Fuxiao of Dalu, Gao Dajing of Shanghai Trust, Chen Liting of Jincheng, Luo Qinghua of Silk, Wang Tianshen of Zhongxing, Tang Mingsan of Overseas Chinese Trust, Chen Runshui of Tongyuan, and Lin Kanghou, Secretary-General of the Banking Association.

Agreed Measures

Chen Guangfu, the chairman, first delivered a welcoming speech, followed by a report from Secretary-General Lin Kanghou on the circumstances of the various meetings of the Banking Association after the National Government promulgated the Savings Bank Law and ordered all banks to implement it immediately, as well as the provisions of Article 9 of the law. A discussion followed, and the following resolutions were passed: (1) Unanimous agreement to adhere to the principles of the Savings Bank Law; (2) Requesting amendments to provisions of the law that are difficult to implement; (3) Temporarily suspending implementation until amendments are made. It was also decided that the Banking Association would send copies of the telegram to the Executive Yuan, Legislative Yuan, and Ministry of Finance, along with the full text of the Savings Bank Law, to all member banks, non-member banks, savings associations, and trust companies within three days to solicit opinions. If the wording is deemed unnecessary to be amended, the Banking Association will then revise it, send it to all non-member banks, savings associations, and trust companies for sealing, and then send it out. The meeting adjourned at 6 PM, with everyone in high spirits.

Government's Views

A reporter from the New Sound News Agency inquired yesterday about the Ministry of Finance's views on the banking sector's request to amend the Savings Bank Law: (1) The Ministry of Finance is an executive body, not a legislative body. Since the National Government promulgated and implemented the law, the Ministry of Finance can only submit the banking sector's opinions to the Executive Yuan to consult the Legislative Yuan for further study. (2) It has been ordered that all banks, in accordance with Article 9 of the Savings Bank Law, deposit government bonds equivalent to one-quarter of the total amount of savings deposits in a special vault set up by the Central Bank as collateral for the repayment of savings deposits. However, the banking sector has requested to use other assets as collateral. This point will be considered. According to the Ministry of Finance's investigation, fixed-term deposits account for 60% of the total deposits in each bank, while current deposits account for 40%. Although one or two banks have current deposits exceeding fixed-term deposits, they are in the minority. Therefore, depositing one-quarter of the security deposit is not difficult. (3) Banks depositing one-quarter of the total savings deposits in government bonds with the Central Bank to maintain credibility could be done by inviting the banks to participate in the organization and management of the vault by the Central Bank.

A dispatch from Nanjing states that the Executive Yuan has received a petition from the Shanghai Banking Association requesting amendments to the Savings Bank Law and will forward it to the Legislative Yuan for handling. According to the Ministry of Finance, the banking sector sent representatives to participate in drafting the law, and there should be no major difficulties. It seems unnecessary to make amendments just after the law has been implemented. As for Article 9, which stipulates that each bank should purchase government bonds equivalent to one-quarter of its savings deposits and hand them over to the Central Bank for safekeeping, it will still be strictly implemented and is difficult to change.

Reopening After Five Years of Suspension

Agricultural and Commercial Bank to Resume Operations

Old Shares Converted and 3 Million New Shares Added

Head Office Established in Shanghai to Issue Banknotes

Shanghai and Hankou Branches to Open on the 15th of This Month

The New Sound News Agency reports that the government-private joint venture Agricultural and Commercial Bank, which suspended operations in March 1929, is now planning to increase its capital and resume operations under the Ministry of Industry. The head office will be located in Shanghai, with branches established in various locations. Details are as follows:

History of the Agricultural and Commercial Bank

The Agricultural and Commercial Bank was founded in 1923 by Gao Lingwei, then Minister of Agriculture and Commerce. The head office was located in Beijing, and the manager was Mr. Jin Caisheng. Branches were established in Shanghai and Tianjin. The paid-up capital was 1,731,000 yuan, and banknotes were issued. It was a government-private joint venture. In March 1929, the bank suspended operations, and all branches were ordered to close. The banknotes issued in Shanghai were all redeemed at face value.

Implementation of Resumption

Chen Gongbo, the Minister of Industry, planned to revive the Agricultural and Commercial Bank, and dispatched the Chief of General Affairs, Mei Zhezhi, to make preparations and increase shareholders. Preparations are now complete, and operations will be resumed. It will still be a government-private joint venture. The former share capital has been converted to 800,000 yuan, and 2,200,000 yuan in new shares have been issued, totaling 3,000,000 yuan. All shares have been fully subscribed. The registration has been submitted and approved by the Ministry of Finance and the Ministry of Industry, and a business license has been issued, along with permission to issue convertible notes.

Organization Details

The head office of the Agricultural and Commercial Bank is located at No. 515, Henan Road, near Ningbo Road, Shanghai. The board of directors consists of 15 members: Chen Gongbo (Chairman), Jiang Danning, Cheng Hejun, Liu Fuxuan, Zhang Rongchu, Mei Zhezhi, Wang Tiesheng, Tang Feifan, Liang Junhua, He Zhuoxian, Mei Jingxiang, Liu Bangrui, Chen Haiqiu, and Wu Ruiyuan. Mei Zhezhi will serve as the general manager. Branches are being prepared for establishment in Shanghai and Hankou first. Locations such as Beijing and Tianjin are still in progress.

Branch Openings

The Shanghai and Hankou branches have been prepared and are scheduled to open simultaneously on the 15th of this month. The notice is as follows: "Our bank has collected a capital of 3 million yuan and has been approved and registered by the Ministry of Finance and the Ministry of Industry, and a business license has been issued. We have also been granted permission to issue convertible notes. We are scheduled to open for business on August 15th. This notice is hereby given." The Shanghai branch is located at the intersection of Henan Road and Ningbo Road, in the same location as the head office.

Banknote Issuance

After the government approved the Agricultural and Commercial Bank to issue banknotes, it decided to issue the banknotes that had been printed but not yet issued by the former Agricultural and Commercial Bank, in denominations of one yuan, five yuan, and ten yuan. The previously printed banknotes have been collected from Beijing by representatives from the head office and will be distributed to the Shanghai and Hankou branches for issuance.

Report to Beijing

General Manager Mei Zhezhi has decided to resign from his position as Chief of General Affairs of the Ministry of Industry in order to devote himself to the affairs of the Agricultural and Commercial Bank. As the Shanghai and Hankou branches are scheduled to open, he took the Beijing-Shanghai overnight express train to Beijing the night before last to report to the Minister. He is scheduled to return to Shanghai in the next day or two. Minister Chen Gongbo is scheduled to come to Shanghai from Beijing to attend the opening of the Shanghai branch.

Shen Hsin Textile Corporation

Established Improvement Committee

Rong Weiren Appointed Chairman and Has Begun Work

Supervisory Committee Formed by Creditor Banks

Experts to Be Hired to Design and Organize Various Factories

The New Sound News Agency reports that Rong Zongjing, the general manager of Shen Hsin Textile Corporation, has established an improvement committee and a supervisory committee, and will hire experts to design and organize the Shen Hsin factories since returning to his post. Details are as follows:

Establishment of Improvement Committee

Rong Zongjing, the general manager of Shen Hsin Textile Corporation, has established an improvement committee for the purpose of self-organization. Rong Weiren, Rong Zongjing's nephew, has been appointed as the chairman. The committee consists of fifteen members, comprising managers from various factories and senior personnel from the head office. The committee is divided into three groups: general affairs, business, and factory affairs. The general affairs group has three members, the business group has four members, and the factory affairs group has four members. It has been formally established and is located in the head office on Jiangxi Road.

Formation of Supervisory Committee

After the establishment of the improvement committee, it was decided to establish a supervisory committee. The number of committee members has also been internally determined and will be formally established soon. The supervisory committee members will be appointed by creditor banks, such as the Bank of China and the Bank of Shanghai. The purpose is to supervise the business development of the various factories under the Shen Hsin Textile Corporation. Experts in the textile industry will be hired to assist in the design and organization. The selection of experts is currently underway.

Soaring Rice Prices for Consecutive Days

Already Exceeded the Thirteen Yuan Price Limit

Bean and Rice Industry Guild Held a Meeting Yesterday

The Great Republic News Agency reports that due to the persistent drought in recent days and the scarcity of rice supplies from the interior, rice prices have been soaring for consecutive days. Top-grade white rice has already exceeded thirteen yuan. The Bean and Rice Industry Guild held an emergency executive and supervisory meeting yesterday, reiterating the price restriction. The Municipal Bureau of Social Affairs also dispatched personnel to investigate rice merchants and prevent price gouging. The actual amount of imported rice ordered by the banking industry and rice merchants has reached over 400,000 piculs. Details are as follows:

Rice Prices Soar Beyond Price Limit

Since the change in weather around the 17th and 18th of last month in this city, with successive showers, rice prices gradually declined. Top-grade white rice from Changshu and Wuxi had dropped from thirteen yuan to twelve yuan at the customs. Public morale was slightly eased. However, in the recent week, the drought returned, and rice prices in this city have soared again. Yesterday, in the North and South city rice markets, second-grade rice from Tongli was priced at twelve yuan and sixty-seven cents. Although the market price of top-grade white rice from the Xichang region remained at thirteen yuan, transactions were secretly inflated by five cents to one yuan. In fact, it has exceeded the price limit. In the past two days, Indica rice and imported rice have each risen by seven or eight cents daily, and there is still a trend of continued price increases.

Emergency Meeting to Warn Fellow Traders

The Bean and Rice Industry Guild held a special emergency meeting yesterday at Cuixiu Hall. Gu Xinyi, Jiang Zisheng, Zhu Yunchang, Lu Jing

German Consulate General

Memorial Service for the Late President Tonight

At 6 PM in the German Church

All German Residents in Shanghai to Attend and Pay Respects

The German Consul General in Shanghai, Klieber, has scheduled a memorial service for the late President Hindenburg tonight at 6 PM in the square of the German Church at the corner of Haig Road and Great Western Road. Mayor Wu, leaders of various organizations, and consuls and military attaches from various countries have been invited to attend. The service will follow a religious ceremony, and all German residents in Shanghai will attend to pay their final respects.

de, Wen Fuqian, Yin Huancun, Ye Tingfan, Fu Changyu, Luo Rongzhou, Cai Yukun, Jiang Hongbin, and Chen Yuming attended. Chaired by Gu Xinyi, the following resolutions were made: (1) Regarding the recent upward trend in rice prices, and how to restrict it, it was resolved to reiterate the previous resolution and notify fellow traders that the highest price for white rice, under any circumstances, must not exceed thirteen yuan. (2) Regarding the establishment of accurate statistics for imported rice orders, it was resolved that all traders who order imported rice must first report and register in detail with the Bureau of Social Affairs and other grain guilds for unified control. After the meeting, an emergency notice was issued, stating that the guild had convened a temporary members' meeting on July 15th and resolved that the highest price for white rice should not exceed thirteen yuan, with corresponding prices for other grades. In addition to notifying all traders to comply, the matter was also reported to the Municipal Bureau of Social Affairs. However, the recent weather has been extremely dry, and the source of rice is not abundant, leading to an upward trend in rice prices. In order to suppress rice prices and maintain the food supply for the people, this guild hereby reiterates the previous resolution, urging all traders to pay attention. The highest price for white rice, under any circumstances, must not exceed thirteen yuan. Otherwise, if discovered by the authorities, this guild cannot be held responsible. This is a special notice.

Bureau of Social Affairs to Dispatch Personnel to Prevent Price Gouging

The Bureau of Social Affairs is paying close attention to the soaring rice prices, which affect the food supply for the people. After receiving news yesterday that top-grade white rice had exceeded thirteen yuan, the head of the Fourth Section, Zhang Binghui, immediately inquired about the truth from Gu Xinyi, chairman of the Bean and Rice Industry Guild, at 10 AM. In addition to formally issuing an order based on the previous resolution passed at the Grain Conference, which restricted rice prices from exceeding thirteen yuan, Grain Section Chief Zhou Minggang was also dispatched to conduct investigations and prevent rice merchants from raising market prices at any time.

The Central News Agency reports that although the Municipal Bureau of Social Affairs has ordered rice merchants to restrict rice prices and not exceed thirteen yuan due to the recent surge in rice prices, it is feared that rice prices will continue to rise based on the current situation. Therefore, it is planned to jointly investigate rice reserves in various regions with the governments of Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces and request transportation agencies to prioritize transporting rice reserves from various regions to Shanghai to suppress rice prices. Regarding the matter of ordering imported rice, if it is determined that domestic rice reserves are indeed lacking, the bureau will consult with the governments of the two provinces to request instructions from the central government for handling. The bureau has already submitted these opinions to the municipal government for forwarding to the governments of Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces for joint consultation and handling.

Registration for Ordering Imported Rice

At the previous grain conference convened by the Bureau of Social Affairs, it was decided that after investigating domestic grain reserves, rice merchants should voluntarily order imported rice and register with the Bureau of Social Affairs. However, rice merchants only know how to seek profits. The city's banking industry and rice merchants have already ordered the first batch of 160,000 piculs of imported rice. According to the Great Republic News Agency reporter's investigation from various sources, another second batch of approximately 250,000 piculs of imported rice was ordered yesterday and today, totaling over 400,000 piculs. The Bean and Rice Industry Guild of this city fears that the market will be filled with imported rice in the future, which will harm the livelihoods of farmers. Therefore, it has specially requested the Bureau of Social Affairs to handle registration and restrict the quantity of imported rice ordered.

Chinese Red Cross Society

Scheduled to Hold National Congress

From September 23rd to 28th

Also, Re-electing the Fourth Board of Directors and Supervisors

The Chinese Red Cross Society General Headquarters at the Continental Marketplace on Second Avenue has 438 branches throughout the country, specializing in wartime rescue of wounded soldiers and refugees, as well as handling relief and all charitable affairs for society, achieving remarkable results. It is learned that the association has been approved by the Ministry of Interior to hold the Fourth National Congress of Members' Representatives in Shanghai from September 23rd to 28th this year. The attendance of representatives is stipulated as one representative for each branch with 30 or more members, and two representatives for 60 or more members, and so on. At that time, 29 directors and 29 supervisors will also be re-elected. The congress budget of 20,000 yuan has been submitted to the Ministry of Interior for approval and allocation. According to a reporter from the National News Agency, there are many preparatory proposals for this congress, which are very important because there is fear that the World War will break out soon. Therefore, the association has decided to expand its affairs in a timely manner, prepare a large amount of medicines, stretchers, flags, etc., and plans to recruit 100,000 male and female paramedics, organize them into teams, and train them to deal with rescue work in an emergency. It is heard that this is the first congress convened since the association was directly administered by the Ministry of Interior of the National Government. As of yesterday, more than 200 branches had registered. Based on the registered branches, the association has been busy preparing and sending out congress admission certificates and ballots in recent days. At the same time, it has reported to the Ministry of Interior to send personnel to guide and supervise the election, and requested the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, the Ministry of Military Affairs, the Ministry of Navy, etc., to send personnel to attend and guide.

National Products Promotion Association Cables Guangdong

Abolish Special Import Tax on National Products from Outside the Province

The Shanghai Citizens' National Products Promotion Association has repeatedly received reports from member factories of cosmetics, enamel, paint, steel, hardware, rubber, matchsticks, and the China Chemical Industry Association that the Guangdong industry and commerce sectors, on the pretext that Shanghai's national product factories have many foreign investments, are dumping goods in Guangdong and are trying their best to persuade the authorities to implement taxes in order to protect the province's industry. It is heard that the authorities have approved their request, convened a local chamber of commerce meeting, and decided to set up a bureau to collect special import taxes on imported goods and national products from outside the province, hindering the promotion of national products. It is learned that the association's promotion of national products has been making rapid progress, and it is struggling to resist the encirclement and attack of foreign goods. The Guangdong industry and commerce sectors have adopted the Monroe Doctrine, ignoring the facts and encouraging the authorities to levy import taxes on national products, treating them the same as imported goods, which has a significant impact on the future of national product promotion, especially the promotion of Shanghai's national product factories' sales in South China. In addition to submitting it to the Standing Committee for consultation and relief, the secretariat yesterday telegraphed the Guangdong provincial financial authorities, stating the advantages and disadvantages, and requesting the cancellation of the original proposal to levy a special import tax on national products from outside the province in order to protect national products.

The Central News Agency reports that Mr. Wang Kemin, Chief Counselor of the Administrative Yuan's Political Consolidation Committee stationed in Peiping, has repeatedly delayed his trip to Qingdao due to waiting for a telegram from Chairman Huang. It is learned that Mr. Wang received a telegram from Mr. Huang on the morning of the 6th, so he decided to leave Shanghai for Qingdao on the morning of the 7th at 9 AM aboard the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's Pu'an. Mr. Wang's trip is solely in response to the telegram invitation from Mr. Song Ziwen, Standing Committee Member of the National Economic Council. It is expected that after arriving in Qingdao, he will stay overnight and then change trains to Peiping.

Public Concession

Rickshaw Dispute Resolved

The Municipal Council Held a Bilateral Meeting Yesterday and Reached a Decision

Rickshaw Merchants in the Special District to Receive New Licenses with Certificates Starting Today

New Regulations to Be Implemented on the 13th, and a Mutual Aid Fund Custodian Committee to Be Established

The New News Agency reports that the rickshaw issue in the Public Concession has been ongoing for nearly a month since the dispute between the Rickshaw Committee and the rickshaw merchants began. To prevent the dispute from escalating, the Municipal Council held a bilateral meeting between the Rickshaw Committee and the rickshaw merchants yesterday morning to discuss various issues and reached considerable results. Rickshaw merchants in the Special District will receive licenses starting today, and the new regulations of the Municipal Council will be implemented on the 13th. Thus, the month-long rickshaw issue can be resolved smoothly. Details are as follows:

The Course of the Dispute

The Public Concession Municipal Council announced that it would implement new regulations from August 1st based on the recommendations of the Rickshaw Affairs Committee. The rickshaw owners and pullers believed that it would greatly harm their interests. The Special District Office of the Rickshaw Industry Guild repeatedly negotiated with the Municipal Council for an extension, but it was ineffective. Therefore, the rickshaw merchants did not receive the August licenses (10,000). The Rickshaw Committee planned to solicit new rickshaw owners, and both sides were tending toward extremes, making the situation very serious. If it had not been resolved yesterday morning, all the rickshaw merchants in the city would have suspended business, which would have affected the livelihoods of more than 100,000 rickshaw pullers. Fortunately, in addition to sending letters to the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce, the Taxpayers' Association, and the Municipal Government for assistance, the industry guild also sent representatives, such as Yin Zhiling, to contact Zhong Si, the Director-General of the Municipal Council, to discuss resolving the dispute between the rickshaw merchants and the Rickshaw Committee to prevent it from escalating and affecting the livelihoods of more than 100,000 rickshaw pullers and ensuring local stability. A meeting was held at the Municipal Council conference room at 3 PM last Friday afternoon, but no concrete results were achieved. It was not until yesterday's second meeting that the issue was completely resolved.

Bilateral Meeting

The Municipal Council convened a second bilateral meeting yesterday morning at 10 AM in the Municipal Council Building, Room 140 on the second floor. The Municipal Council was represented by Director-General Zhong Si, Chief Inspector McDing, Rickshaw Committee Director Massey, Chinese Director Yu Qiaqing, and Associate He De Kui. The rickshaw merchants were represented by Yin Zhiling, Gu Songmao, Hou Shao'an, Mark Shi, Pei Er, and Cheng Xiechun, Chairman of the Jianghuai Fellow Villagers Association, totaling twelve people. The meeting was chaired by Zhong Si and recorded by Bailang. First, the rickshaw merchants' representatives submitted eight proposed opinions in writing for discussion. The two sides debated fiercely and then adopted a voting system. The majority agreed (the New Voice News Agency reported that only Massey opposed) as the resolutions. The meeting adjourned at 1:15 PM.

Eight Opinions

Yesterday, the rickshaw merchants' representatives submitted eight specific opinions in writing to the representatives. The following is a verbatim record: (1) The new regulations of the Municipal Council, which are to be implemented from August, stipulate that the rent for publicly licensed rickshaws in the Public Concession should be 10 cents per day per vehicle, and the rickshaw owner should pay a mutual aid fee of 1.5 yuan per month per vehicle, and an additional 1 cent per day should be collected from the rickshaw puller. The rickshaw merchants are willing to reduce the rent from 14 cents to 12 cents per day per vehicle from the date of the new license in August, including the benefits of contractors and the licenses of the Chinese, French, and British concessions. (2) In addition, the rickshaw owner will voluntarily pay 1 yuan per month per vehicle for the rickshaw puller's relief fund, which will be transferred by the rickshaw merchants' guild to nine directors for safekeeping, subject to the supervision of the Municipal Council. (3) The improvement of rickshaws should be done in cooperation with the rickshaw merchants' guild and should focus on solidity, cleanliness, and economy, rather than being flashy, so as not to increase the burden on rickshaw pullers and passengers. (4) The operation of publicly licensed rickshaws is not a simple undertaking. The first and second paragraphs of the new license regulations should be amended as follows: (a) The licensee (individual or company) should be the owner of the licensed vehicle. (b) If the licensee wishes to transfer the operation of the publicly licensed rickshaw to someone else, they should report the details and the number of licenses to the Municipal Council. (5) Rickshaw merchants need capital to prepare vehicles to obtain a license to operate, so they should have considerable security to continue operating. Therefore, the last paragraph of the third item of the new regulations should be deleted. (6) The rickshaw puller's licensing regulations and the implementation of the new regulations, such as items 10, 11, 12, 16, 17, and 18, impose many difficulties on the rickshaw owners and should be carefully revised. (7) The registration and certification of genuine rickshaw owners are matters of property rights, which must be handled with caution. The rickshaw merchants' guild and the donors will cooperate with the Municipal Council to complete it within the time limit to avoid omissions and damage to the interests of genuine rickshaw owners. However, before the completion within the time limit, the license should be issued to the donors, who will be responsible for maintaining the Municipal Council's collection of donations from rickshaw owners and social stability. (8) To consider the rickshaw merchants' guild's recommendations and implement the new regulations effectively, a special committee on the rickshaw industry should be established, composed of five to seven representatives jointly appointed by the Municipal Council and the rickshaw merchants' guild. This committee will serve as an advisory body to the Municipal Council's rickshaw affairs agency.

Solution

The following solutions were resolved at yesterday's meeting: (1) Rickshaw merchants face the Municipal Council's decision to charge 10 cents per day for vehicles with Public Concession licenses from August 1st, with a 1 cent mutual aid fee and a prepayment of 1.5 yuan per month by the rickshaw merchants, changed to a total of 12 cents, including the licenses of the Chinese, British, and French concessions and the contractor's remuneration. (Resolution) The rent for each vehicle per day is changed to 7.8 cents, with a 0.7 cent mutual aid fee, and the rickshaw merchants will prepay 1.5 yuan per vehicle per month for the mutual aid fund, starting from August 15th. (2) The improvement of rickshaw design must solicit the opinions of rickshaw merchants and focus on solidity, cleanliness, and hygiene, not flashy design. (Resolution) Passed. (3) Rickshaw owners' certification will be extended from today to August 13th. The rickshaw merchants' guild will send personnel to assist rickshaw owners in obtaining certification and paying donations. The guild will pay 15,000 yuan for the mutual aid fee for this month. For those whose ownership has not been determined and for whom certificates cannot be issued, they are allowed to operate with their old licenses until the end of the month in order to resolve the dispute. (4) Rickshaw pullers' registration is a major issue. (Resolution) Reserved for further discussion and implementation. (5) The chairman explained that items 2 and 3 of the new regulations, regarding the rickshaw owner's property rights protection, do not harm the rickshaw pullers' legal interests. (6) Establishment of the mutual aid fund custodian committee, number of members. (Resolution) 15 people, 3 foreigners, and 12 Chinese. The rickshaw merchants will recommend two representatives, and the other three directors will be temporarily appointed by the Rickshaw Committee for a trial period of eight months, because the Rickshaw Committee established by the Municipal Council is also temporary in nature.

Licenses to Be Issued Today

The New Voice News Agency reports that the Municipal Council will issue 10,000 rickshaw licenses for this month in the Public Concession only after handling the rickshaw owners' certification and complying with the new regulations, which was unsatisfactory to all rickshaw owners, so they have not been issued yet. Now that the dispute has been resolved, the rickshaw owners have decided to start receiving them today, and the Municipal Council has also decided to issue them today. The Rickshaw Industry Guild of the Special District held a temporary board meeting at 7 PM last night. Yin Zhiling, Gu Songmao, Hou Shao'an, etc., attended. The representatives who attended the Municipal Council meeting reported on the meeting process and the solution. It was resolved that the guild would send personnel to assist in obtaining the licenses from the Rickshaw Committee.

Relationship Between People's Needs and Politics

Mayor Wu's Speech at the Commemoration Week

The Central News Agency reports that the Shanghai Municipal Government held a commemoration week yesterday. After Mayor Wu Tiecheng led the ceremony, he reported on "The Relationship Between People's Needs and Politics," stating: "Fellow comrades, there was a famous political scholar in ancient Western history, Plato, who once said, 'The creation of the state is due to the need to meet economic needs. An isolated person wants to use his own strength to meet his own needs and achieve a perfect life, which is absolutely impossible in reality. Therefore, it is necessary to rely on society, rely on the cooperation of the majority.' Everyone knows that Plato's thought directly originated from Socrates. Socrates also said about the origin of the state, 'The state is born to meet human needs. Humans have many needs, and no one can provide for themselves. People must help each other to meet each other's needs. This person needs help for this purpose, and that person needs help for that purpose. When these people who help each other live together, the state is born. At this time, mankind begins to have the concept of the state. Therefore, the true creator of the state is "need." (Necessity)' I often think to myself that whatever we do, we cannot succeed with one person's hands and feet. We must gain the sympathy and practical support and cooperation of the majority. Then this thing can succeed, whether it is a public matter or a private matter, I think there can be no exceptions. Especially for our government authorities, in China today, when everything is waiting to be done, how should we think about awakening the people, so that the people can express sympathy for the government? But if we only gain the sympathy of the people and cannot gain the support and cooperation of the people, our politics still cannot be developed much. The political desire of the Chinese people has always been very small, because Chinese politics in the past was mostly passive, so the people developed a habit of being very passive towards politics. Because the people are passive towards politics, it makes it difficult for politics to actively seek development. Therefore, it is not enough for us to only gain the sympathy of the people. In addition to working hard to make the people express sympathy for us, we must also work hard to make them take their strength to help us and cooperate with us. In this way, when the Chinese government authorities, in this time when everything is waiting to be done, want to do something, it can be done and there is hope of success. How can we enable the people to practically help us and cooperate with us? One thing we should know is "need." If the people can know the needs of the country today, the people will definitely be able to help the government and cooperate with the government to build the country. Therefore, our urgent task today is to make the people know the needs of the country and society today. The two words "need" can be said to be the power of human happiness and the advancement of world civilization today. Because of this human need, the world has today's advanced civilization, and all mankind has gained today's happiness. Therefore, need is the driving force of human evolution and the creative power of world culture.

This theory of mine is not inherited from the old ideas of Western scholars, but there is a very obvious example to support it. We only need to look at the construction of Guangzhou and Shanghai to know. First, let's talk about Shanghai. Shanghai has a population of about 3 million, and two-fifths of them live in the Special District. These two-fifths of the citizens are the most powerful people in the city. There are many who are enthusiastic about supporting the government and participating in construction, but some people think that their lives and property are protected, and their "desire for life" is satisfied, so they often ignore and do not pay much attention to the undertakings needed by the general citizens outside the Special District. But Guangzhou is slightly different. Although Guangzhou also has concessions, the so-called concession "Shameen" is very small and Chinese people are not allowed to live there. Therefore, the people of Guangzhou all live in Guangzhou, where they were born and raised. Therefore, they have a common need with the government, and they can do their best to help the government and cooperate with the government to build the city and revitalize it. That is why Guangzhou has today's construction achievements. This is an excellent example of the relationship between need and politics. Therefore, the most important thing for our government authorities is to become a clean government, not to be corrupt and pervert the law. Everyone should be a good official in order to win the sympathy of the people. But because we want to do things actively and build actively, the sympathy of the people is not enough. We must also make the people know their living needs. If the people can know their living needs, their desire for life can be expanded considerably, and they can naturally participate in and support all the construction undertakings of the government in a practical way and cooperate with the government. In this way, any thing our government wants to do, whether big or small, can have a hope of success.

Speaking of this, I feel that there is a very great need in this city that should be carried out as soon as possible, which is the construction of public housing, which was announced two months ago. I often say and often hear people say that there are so-called phenomena of national decline and national prosperity, phenomena of family decline and family prosperity. But where can these phenomena be seen? They can be seen in the lives of the general public. Therefore, Chairman Chiang promotes the New Life Movement, not only to improve the living desire of the general public in a negative way, but it can be said that the greatest purpose of the New Life Movement is to make the people know their needs. If the people can know their needs, they will definitely be able to aspire to work hard, and they will definitely be able to take all their strength, directly or indirectly, alone or jointly, to create and participate in all the needed undertakings in order to satisfy their desire for life. In this way, a country or a nation can be revived. Therefore, I think now that we should combine the strength of the entire Shanghai to build public housing. We know that there are about 30,000 thatched houses in Shanghai. On average, five people live in each thatched house, so there are a total of 150,000 people living in thatched houses. These 150,000 people live in poverty, irregularity, irrationality, unsanitary conditions, and unhealthy lives every day. This kind of life not only affects the city's appearance, public security, and public health, etc., but also makes it difficult to start civic education. Therefore, if we want to improve the lives of the common people, it is very easy to do it in a negative way, it is not difficult, or if we only use political power to do it, we can get some results, but this effect is temporary, not permanent, because we have not fundamentally increased their living knowledge, expanded their living attitude, made them know their needs, and enabled them to improve their own lives in practice. Therefore, the purpose of our building public housing is, in a negative way, to improve their lives, so that 150,000 common people in Shanghai can live in a better place and lead a more rational, regular, and healthier life. In a positive way, we can also carry out various civic education, increase their knowledge, increase their desire for life, and enable people to aspire to work hard and become very powerful citizens. Therefore, the effectiveness of building public housing is not only negative, it can solve the problems of the city's appearance, public security, public health, civic education, etc. At the same time, because their lives have improved and their living knowledge has increased, they can more actively know greater needs and be able to actively strive to jointly solve major urban problems and seek urban prosperity. In short, the people's "needs" are very related to what our government does. If the people can know their "needs," they will not only be able to sympathize with our construction, but also be able to practically participate in and help our construction. But how to make the people know their needs and support us is still what we should strive for in China today, when everything is waiting to be done.

Private Cigarette Suppression Association Established Yesterday

Bao Gengsheng and Others Elected as Standing Committee Members

The Private Cigarette Suppression Assistance Committee held its inaugural meeting at the Taxation Department of the Ministry of Finance on Hankou Road yesterday at 3:00 PM. Attendees included Wu Qiding, Chen Shaoji, Chen Zhongpei, Dong Zhongding, Wang Zongzhu, Tang Shi, Han Gong, Jiang Yongyi, Bao Gengsheng, Shen Weiting, Lao Jingxiu, Sun Lishan, Chen Maonan, Shen Kunyu, and Li Xuedong. Observers included Wu Tingsheng. Chairman Wu Qiding presided over the meeting, which proceeded according to protocol. First, the Chairman gave a report, stating briefly that today was the establishment of the association. In order to reorganize cigarette tax revenue and promote the development of cigarette manufacturers' business, the association adhered to the principle of cooperation between officials and merchants, and would strive to carry out suppression of smuggling. He hoped that all colleagues would work hard for the country and society. Next, the meeting passed the constitution, organizational law, and the allocation of funds. Then, a proposal was discussed: (1) A proposal to publicly decide on the custody and requisition procedures for suppression funds. It was resolved that the suppression funds would be kept in the custody of the association, and the requisition procedures would be valid only with the signatures of one full-time and one part-time person. (2) A proposal to publicly decide on where to locate the association's office. It was resolved that the association's office would be temporarily located at the Shanghai Chinese Cigarette Manufacturers Association on Mei Bai Ge Road. (3) A proposal to publicly decide on which day of the month would be appropriate for the association to hold a standing committee meeting once a month. It was resolved that the most appropriate date for the standing committee meeting would be the first Wednesday of each month. Immediately afterwards, the election of the standing committee began. Bao Gengsheng and Shen Weiting (full-time) were elected from the cigarette merchant side, and Chen Shaoji and Chen Zhongpei were elected from the tax side. The meeting adjourned after the election.

Pudong Kaiping Warehouse Carelessly

Coal Baskets Easily Ignite, Fire Raged

The coal basket warehouse of Pudong's Eighteen Jian Kaiping Coal Yard suddenly caught fire carelessly at around 11:00 PM last night. The coal baskets were easily flammable, so the fire spread quickly. In an instant, the fire illuminated the sky, making it impossible to approach. The nearby third district, second division learned of this and quickly notified the fire brigade, dispatching fire trucks to the scene to put out the fire. At the same time, the Pudong fireboat also sailed to assist in dousing the flames. Unfortunately, the weather was dry and it was easy for the fire to catch, so the fire actually increased rather than decreased. By midnight this morning, it had not subsided at all. As for how the fire started and how much damage was done, since it was late at night and the fire was raging, it was impossible to find out at the time.

Illegal Sauce Garden Sealed

Chen Junfa Commits Suicide in Desperation

Chen Junfa from Shaoxing, 29 years old, worked as a tea servant in the China Enterprise Bank's dormitory located at No. 84 Mingde Lane, Fuxu Road. He had always been diligent and thrifty and had saved up some money. He opened Bao Kang Sauce Garden at the intersection of Aiweniyi Road and Mei Baike Road in the Public Concession, and had been open for business for sixteen days. Because the store sold wine without obtaining a license issued by the工部局, it was ordered to close by the工部局. After repeated attempts to request one, it was ultimately difficult to obtain this license because it did not meet sanitary regulations, and he could not continue to operate. All of his capital, several hundred yuan, was completely exhausted. In desperation, he had a sudden thought and bought Lysol solution. Yesterday morning at around 8:00 AM, he swallowed it in the亭子間 of the Enterprise Bank dormitory and committed suicide. At noon, his companions urged him to have lunch, and that's when they discovered what happened. He was immediately sent to the Red Cross Hospital on Haige Road, but because he had been poisoned so deeply, treatment was ineffective, and he died at 1:45 PM. The hospital reported to the police, who sent detectives to investigate the circumstances of the deceased's suicide. Meanwhile, the body was transported by car to the Tongren Fuyuan branch morgue for an autopsy. The case will be reported to the Second Special District Court today to send personnel to examine it.

Rickshaw Puller Angry Wife Doesn't Return

Self-Harm by Undressing in Court

Stabbing Chest with Knife, Blood Flows Freely

Egg Means Rolling Away Pear Means Separation

丨Rickshaw Puller Says Wife Intended to Flee丨

Yang Chaoyuan, 24 years old, from Funing, lives in a shed on Gonghe Road and makes a living pulling a rickshaw. Last October, he married Ms. Xu, a fellow villager and adopted daughter of Qian Guoyan (who raised her after she lost her parents). Ms. Xu is 17 years old. They married on February 5th of the lunar calendar this year. After arriving, she often returned to Ning for various reasons. Yang Chaoyuan repeatedly dissuaded her, but not only did she not listen, she intensified her actions, sometimes not returning until late. As a result, the couple's relationship was broken. In early May, Ms. Xu returned to her mother's home again. Every time she left and returned, his attempts were ineffective. Yang Chaoyuan is a coolie who finds it difficult to marry a wife. He often tells people that it cost him more than 400 yuan to marry Ms. Xu, resulting in a mountain of debt. This time, she left without saying goodbye, and he couldn't find her. It was like releasing a white dove. Therefore, he hired someone to write a complaint and filed a lawsuit against Xu Guoyan and Ms. Xu for handing over the person. Yesterday morning, Judge He Jingxian specially opened the fourth court to hear the case. Xu Guoyan was absent, and only Ms. Xu appeared in court, claiming that her daughter was beaten and driven out by Yang Chaoyuan and did not return home. Yang Chaoyuan then testified about what had happened before. He was filled with anger and immediately took out a knife (a foot knife) from his sleeve and undressed in court, stabbing his chest deeply. Blood flowed freely. The judge caught sight of this and quickly ordered the court bailiffs to take the knife away and take him to the prosecutor's office for sealing. After the prosecutor examined him, because the injury was not light, he immediately ordered him to be sent to the hospital for treatment. The knife was confiscated. According to Yang Chaoyuan, Ms. Xu fled before she had been married for 100 days. Before Ms. Xu left, she claimed that her mother gave her an egg when she entered the door (thinking that after 100 days of marriage, the egg would roll away), and used a knife to split a pear (referring to a sign of separation), and cut an onion with a knife (meaning that cutting an onion with a knife is empty at both ends), and put a piece of fresh meat skin into Ms. Xu's pocket and carried it with her when she entered the door (meaning that she could treat her husband like a pig). All of this proves that she had premeditated thoughts and planned to escape. But we poor people are being fooled like this, and both our spirits and money are damaged. It is painful to talk about, so it is better to die than to suffer.

Biological Father

Knife Cuts Biological Child

Eight Children Born, None Survived

Uninformed Laborer Acts Cruelly

In the wasteland at the entrance of Yongqing Lane, Xiaosha Ferry Road, Shanghai West, at 1:00 PM the day before yesterday, a newborn baby boy, about six months old, wrapped in diapers, was suddenly found crying loudly. He was discovered by passers-by. The child was lying in a pool of blood and was immediately reported to the nearby Putuo Road Police Station. Detective Tan Jinhai was dispatched to investigate. The child had knife marks all over his body. There were a total of eight cuts on his face, abdomen, hands, legs, and other parts. The child was immediately sent to Baolong Hospital for treatment. His life was in great danger. After investigation, it was found that the child was born to Yang Yulou, a laborer at the Fufeng Flour Mill at No. 30 Beiyinghua Lane, Robert Sheng Road. Yang was immediately taken to the police station. According to Yang, he and his wife had produced eight children, all of whom died prematurely. None of them survived. This child (the one who was cut) was six months old and suddenly became seriously ill. Therefore, he angrily used a kitchen knife to cut the child eight times, thinking that he was dead, and threw him into the wasteland. He believed that this child had come to collect debts again, since he had not been able to keep any of the eight children he had had. It is a great wonder that he did not die after being stabbed eight times. The police station, because Yang's intentions were vicious and he committed the crime of murder, immediately transferred Yang to the First Special District Court for investigation. The child was left in Baolong Hospital for treatment.

Forging Court Summons

Purpose is to Vent Anger

Result is Getting Caught in the Net of the Law

Zhou Genxing, a Guangdong native residing at No. 6, Qipu Road, recently fell in love with Miao Ying, the daughter of Ms. He Wu of No. 35, Tiantong Road, and lived together. They had a child. Unexpectedly, He's feelings for Zhou suddenly broke down, and in January of this year, she took the child back to her hometown, without a trace. Zhou was anxious and often went to her place to make a fuss, asking her to hand over Miao Ying and his son. However, Ms. He Wu ignored him. In anger, Zhou said that he would sue in court, but fearing that he would not achieve his goal and lose money, and since he was an electrician at the Xieqiao General Assembly on Jing'an Temple Road, he heard that his friend Shou Arong had obtained a summons from the Civil Court of the First Special Court in a money debt case. Zhou then borrowed it and took it to Jiatai Printing House at No. 364, Tiantong Road, and asked his colleague Ding Can, a native of Changzhou, to imitate and print 100 identical fake summons, costing 1 yuan and 8 cents. He asked his colleague Zhu Chengxiang, a tea servant from Shaoxing, to fill in a lawsuit case of Zhou Genxing suing He Miaoying, asking her to go to court to resolve the matter. One summons was also delivered by his colleague Liu Ahai, a tea servant from Ningbo. The case was discovered by Zhao Bingkun, a Chinese detective of the Hongkou Police Station, who arrested Zhou and the other three and sent them to the First Special District Court for questioning. Upon clear instructions, they were ordered to await sentencing. Yesterday, Judge Wu Zehan came to court and announced the sentence.

Proclaiming Aviation to Save the Country

Walking Group Leaves Shanghai for Zhejiang This Morning

Scheduled to Travel Through the Country in Two and a Half Years

Raising Awareness of National Defense, No Donations Along the Way

The China National Aviation Promotion to Save the Country Walking Propaganda Group has completed its propaganda in Shanghai and is scheduled to leave for Zhejiang this morning. The details are as follows:

Propaganda Completed

The organization of the group is composed of anti-Japanese comrades from the Independent Brigade of the Former Northeast National Salvation Army's Frontline Headquarters. After arriving in Shanghai from the Beijing-Shanghai Road in the middle of last month, they have successively conducted written and oral propaganda at the Public Education Hall, Fuan Amusement Park, Gonghe Cinema, and Xiaoshijie, gaining considerable sympathy and approval from all sectors.

Leaving Shanghai for Zhejiang

The group leader Chen Zhenglong and group members Huang Biyuan and others, a total of eleven people, are scheduled to depart from the North Station in Shanghai this morning and walk along the Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway to Zhejiang. They will go to Songjiang, Fengjing, Jiashan, Jiaxing, Xiashi, Chang'an, and Hangzhou, and then go to various counties in Zhejiang Province to conduct propaganda. In major towns and cities, they will stay and conduct propaganda. The main points are: (1) The experience of the Northeast War, (2) The reasons for the failure, (3) The relationship between the air force and national defense. They will stay in Zhejiang for about one or two months.

National Itinerary

The group's planned national itinerary is as follows: after arriving in Hangzhou, they will pass through the entire province and reach Jiangsu, Anhui, Jiangxi, Hubei, Henan, Shanxi, Shaanxi, Gansu, Ningxia, Qinghai, Tibet, Mongolia, Suiyuan, Chahar, Hebei, Shandong, Fujian, Guangdong, Guangxi, Yunnan, Guizhou, Hunan, Sichuan, and then go east along the Yangtze River and enter Beijing. The journey will take a total of two and a half years, ending at the end of 1936. The time may be extended if necessary, so that compatriots can deeply understand before stopping. No donations will be collected along the way.

Defrauding Copper Coins

18,000 Yuan

A Moment's Greed Causes Lifelong Harm

Years of Reputation Lost in an Instant

Sun Yushun, a native of Zhenjiang residing at No. 12, Anlin Lane, Xujiahui Road, French Concession, is 56 years old. He operates Baotai Cigarette Paper Store on Min Guo Road in the French Concession, employing Ye Changshan as manager and Sun Xintang as accountant. He also operates Zhonghua Bathhouse on Shanxi Road, employing Wang Tingzhi as manager, and Dongfang Hotel on Min Guo Road, managed by Chu Lianke. Sun has been trading copper coins with the French Tram Company in Lujiawan for six years. The company, because Sun has multiple stores and a good reputation, has been quite trusting. However, on June 17th of this year, after Sun received 18,000 yuan in copper coins from the Tram Company, he issued a promissory note from Baotai. Immediately, Sun colluded with Ye and Sun to close the store and divide the money, fleeing with it. After learning of this, the Tram Company reported it to the French police, requesting a joint arrest warrant. On the one hand, the Tram Company found out that Sun Yushun had Zhonghua Bathhouse and Dongfang Hotel, and immediately went to negotiate. The managers of the two stores allowed them to pay compensation in full. Until the afternoon of the day before yesterday, the special task force inspector of the French police, Jin Jiulin, detectives Zhang Ziying and Qian Yumin, and deputy detectives Yang Yilong and Bao Tan Wu Wengang, found the third defendant Sun Xintang hiding in the Daji Cigarette Paper Store at No. 1430, Aiduya Road, and immediately rushed there and arrested Sun. Yesterday morning, he was escorted to the 8th Criminal Court of the Second Special District Court. The police lawyer Gu Shouxi said that the police still needed to investigate the case and requested a postponement. Liu Changyin, the comprador of the Tram Company, sent representative Xu Jingshan to the case to clarify the case. After Judge Wu Fanglian verified the confession and questioned Sun Xinben, he approved the postponement for another trial. The defendant was returned to custody.

A Bomb in a Trash Can

Explodes After Pouring in Watermelon Rinds

Lu Afu's Face Blasted

No. 5 Lianyi Lane, Daji Road outside Ximen, is the home of Dr. Xu Zhongen of Tongren Hospital. Yesterday afternoon at around 4:00 PM, male servant Lu Afu, 24 years old, from Tongzhou, was splitting a watermelon in the middle of the hall. After the family finished eating the watermelon, Afu collected the watermelon rinds and everything else and carried them out to pour into the trash can at the entrance of the lane. Unexpectedly, there was a bomb stored in the can. After falling to the ground unconscious, he was sent to Tongren Hospital for treatment by someone.

Former Comprador of Jardine Matheson

Luo Buzhou Falsely Accuses Sister-in-Law of Theft Case

Travels Far to Shanghai to Visit, is Falsely Accused of Theft and Arrested by Police

Widowed Sister-in-Law is Unwilling and Files Lawsuit in Court

丨Two Trials Announced Verdict Yesterday丨

Luo Buzhou (aka Luo Guangying), a native of Xiakou, Hubei, who previously served as a comprador for the British trading company Jardine Matheson in Xiaguan, Nanjing, has been living in a Western-style house at No. 850 Yuyuan Road in this port since retiring from his position as a comprador, enjoying a life of luxury. Luo had an older brother named Ziyuan, who passed away in the winter of 1930. His widowed sister-in-law, Luo Chen Yuzhen, requested that Buzhou divide the jointly owned property, but Buzhou refused. Therefore, Luo Chen filed civil and criminal lawsuits separately in the Hankou District Court. However, Buzhou consistently refused to appear in court, so the lawsuits have been unable to proceed. However, Luo Chen is feeling increasingly distressed and struggling to raise her orphaned child because the property has not been divided.

Recently, she personally went to Buzhou's residence to negotiate the public property issue. She was reported to the Jing'an Temple Police Station by Buzhou, who accused Luo Chen of being a thief. The police station ordered Chinese and Western detectives to go to arrest her. It was then found out that it was a domestic dispute, and she was released. However, Luo Chen was very unwilling to suffer this false accusation and hired lawyers Fan Gang, Lou Ying, and Luo Jiaheng to file a criminal self-accusation against Luo Buzhou in the First Special District District Court, stating that the late husband Ziyuan and the defendant were brothers and had joint property that had not been divided. Unfortunately, Ziyuan passed away. The defendant had sinister intentions and forced the plaintiff's underage son, Mingxiao, to sign his name while the plaintiff was escorting the coffin back to Han for burial. The plaintiff had filed a criminal self-accusation in the Hankou District Court, but it had not been concluded because the defendant was hiding and failing to appear. The plaintiff then thought that they were close relatives and should not continue the lawsuit, and planned to meet with the defendant to explain everything. She once sent her son and daughter-in-law to Shanghai to visit the defendant this spring to convey this message. However, they were turned away. The plaintiff had no choice but to come in person. Since she was unfamiliar with the place, she asked Ms. Ye, who was living with her, to accompany her to the defendant's residence, knock on the door, and request a meeting to state her intentions. Unexpectedly, the defendant not only refused to let her in for a face-to-face meeting, but also privately reported to the police station, falsely accusing the plaintiff of being a robber. The police station, based on the report, immediately ordered detectives to take the plaintiff to the case. The plaintiff asked Luo Guangying

to go to the police station

for questioning at the same time. The detectives said that Luo Guangying reported that you were a robber and should first go to the police station to await investigation. The plaintiff had no choice but to go and be detained. Only after being questioned did the plaintiff explain in detail that she and the defendant were uncle and sister-in-law, and that she had come to visit this time to discuss family matters. She was then released. The defendant falsely accused the plaintiff of being a robber, intending to put her to death in order to achieve his grand plan of encroaching on the joint property. Judging from his behavior, he should be convicted of the crime under Article 180 of the Criminal Law. The plaintiff is a weak woman and is living in a foreign land without any support. The defendant is the younger brother of the plaintiff's deceased husband. If he had a conscience, how should he protect her? Now, he is

falsely accusing his sister-in-law of theft

because of his greed for money. His heart is so cruel that it is unparalleled in the world. Therefore, she was forced to file a self-accusation, hoping that the case would be quickly investigated, the punishment would be strictly enforced, and that the law would be upheld. After being accused, Luo also hired lawyer Wu Kaisheng to submit a statement defending himself, denying that he reported the plaintiff to the police as a thief at the time. He only said that someone came to his house to make a fuss and filed a counterclaim against Luo Chen, saying that she intended to intimidate and extort money. The First Special Court had already summoned him once. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Wu Zehan opened a court session to continue the trial and summoned the Chinese and Western detectives from the Jing'an Temple Police Station who handled the case as witnesses. Judge Wu then questioned both the plaintiff and the defendant in detail about the verbal arguments between the two parties on the 15th and 17th of last month, as well as the process of the defendant reporting to the police. The lawyers from both sides then debated with each other until the end, and the court immediately announced that both Luo Buzhou and Luo Chen Yuzhen were innocent.

On the side of the residence, in the cotton field, he was killed. Later, detectives from the Shanghai Public Security Bureau first arrested the suspect Zhou Ah Yuan from Jiangyin in Shanghai. On the evening of the 29th of the same month, they arrested the main culprit Wang Deyu (26 years old, the deceased's uxorilocal brother) at the Nanyang Quanji Restaurant and brought him to the bureau for interrogation. After investigating, the French police found that the starting point for the deceased being lured out was in the French Concession, so they immediately sent detectives to the Public Security Bureau to transfer the two criminals, Zhou and Wang, to their custody for investigation. They were transferred to the Second Special District District Court and prosecuted for the crime of premeditated murder. At the end of the trial, Wang Deyu was sentenced to death for murder, and Zhou Ah Yuan was found not guilty. Wang Deyu, dissatisfied with the verdict, submitted a statement to the Third Branch of the Jiangsu Higher Court to file an appeal. The details have been reported in the previous newspapers. The Higher Court approved the appeal and opened an investigation court, summoning detectives from the Shanghai and Nanyang Public Security Bureaus, as well as the waiter from the Quanji Restaurant and the police officer in charge of the case, to be interrogated. The day before yesterday, the criminal court Guo Dezhang, together with judges Sun Honglin and Fan Peien, and prosecutor Zhang, opened a joint court to hear the appeal. According to the appellant Wang's statement of appeal reasons, he overturned the confession from the original trial and said that he had no feud with the deceased. Even if he had property, I could not seize it. Even if I killed him, I would not be able to obtain his property. Why should I kill him? The death of Ding Fugen was actually caused by his brother-in-law Tang Ajin. The court verified the confession and ordered a re-examination with scheduled witness summons. The appellant was still detained pending instructions.

China National Aviation Corporation

Opening of Shanghai-Qingdao Summer Special Flight

Round trip once every Saturday and Sunday.

"Shen Shi She" reports that, for the convenience of people in Shanghai to take advantage of Saturdays and Sundays to travel to Qingdao for summer vacation, China National Aviation Corporation has specifically decided to launch a direct Shanghai-Qingdao special flight starting this week, with a scheduled round trip once a week. A reporter from "Shen Shi She" investigated and reported the details as follows:

Shanghai-Qingdao Special Flight

The company, in view of the extremely hot weather and to facilitate those who are professionally bound and cannot easily obtain a long period of leave from Shanghai to escape the summer heat, has specially opened a Shanghai-Qingdao summer special flight, with round trips between Qingdao and Shanghai once every Saturday and Sunday. Those who usually have official duties and cannot travel far from Shanghai can take advantage of their Saturday and Sunday holidays to fly to Qingdao for a one-day and one-night tour, and return to Shanghai the next day. It has now been decided to start implementing this from this week. Those who have booked seats for the flight are very enthusiastic.

Schedule and Prices

The timetable for the Shanghai-Qingdao summer special flight has been finalized as follows: Departure every Saturday at 7:00 AM, arriving in Qingdao at 11:30 AM on the same day, spending the night in Qingdao, and leaving Qingdao on the same plane at 2:00 PM the next afternoon, returning to Shanghai at 6:00 PM. The price for a round-trip ticket is 200 yuan per passenger, and a one-way ticket is 100 yuan.

Huang Jianbai, a Chinese National

Invents "New Boat" for Water Transportation

Safe and with extremely shallow draft

Actively manufacturing in a factory in Shanghai

Huang Jianbai, a native of Hunan Province, has been working at the Guanghua Electric Light Factory in Hunan. Recently, he has been very interested in the shipbuilding industry and has invented a type of "New Boat" for water transportation. Its shape is similar to an airship, travels very fast, and is very safe. The ship is 94 feet long, about 17 feet wide, and 5 feet high, with a displacement of 30 tons and a weight of 30 tons. It uses 106 rectangular floating boxes made of light metal alloy, which are arranged around the bottom and back of the ship from head to tail, supporting the hull. The bottom of the ship is about 6 inches above the water. The test results show that although the speed of the ship is not as fast as an airship, it is extremely safe and labor-saving, and its draft is very shallow, making it most suitable for sailing in inland harbors. He has already applied to the Ministry of Industry and Commerce for registration. Currently, many people in Hunan Province are purchasing them. Mr. Huang wrote to a friend in Shanghai yesterday, planning to set up a large-scale manufacturing plant in Shanghai to actively manufacture them in order to expand the sales scope.

West City Business Community Rent Reduction Meeting

Organizing a meeting to promote the resolution of various key issues.

The shops along Zhonghua Road, Fangxie Road, Heping Road, and Zhaojiabang Road in the Nanshi area feel that business is declining and the situation is not good. The burden of rent is particularly difficult to bear. Since the reconstruction of houses and the widening of roads in Ximen, the market appears to be prosperous on the surface, so the landlords are raising rents. However, the shops are generally operating poorly, and they are outwardly strong but inwardly weak. It is now known that rent reduction movements are actively underway in various places. In order to promote the early realization of rent reduction in a unified manner, the West City shops held a West City Business Community Rent Reduction Promotion Conference at the Mingyuan Restaurant in the area yesterday at 2:00 PM. Here is a summary of various news:

West City Business Community Rent Reduction Promotion Conference. The West City Business Community Rent Reduction Promotion Conference was officially held at 2:00 PM yesterday. More than 100 representatives from the business community attended. Cao Mo, Feng Xueqiao, and Lu Hanjun were publicly elected as the presidium, and Ding Songan was the recorder. After the formalities, Chairman Cao Mo first reported the purpose of the meeting and the significance of the business community's demand for rent reduction. Then, Wang Shenqing, Tong Shijie, Li Sen, Gao Zixin, Huang Lianfu, Gu Zhenxin, Zhao Taidian, Wang Shaoqin, and others successively expressed their opinions. The chairman summarized the various opinions and resolved to pass various action plans, including (1) organizing a rent reduction promotion association, (2) carrying out rent registration for commercial shops and having the association prepare a form, (3) determining the standard for rent reduction in accordance with the regulations of the Shanghai Rent Reduction Committee, (4) issuing a declaration from the business community demanding rent reduction, (5) posting various rent reduction slogans, (6) investigating the names of local landlords and owners in order to send letters to them separately to persuade them to reduce rent automatically, (7) deciding not to pay rent if the rent is not reduced and depositing the original rent in a designated bank, (8) hiring lawyers Wu Kaisheng and Li Ming to form a legal advisory group, (9) all shops should join the West City Business Community Federation to request assistance with rent reduction, and (10) publishing the West City Commercial News to promote the rent reduction movement. The above methods were all approved, and 21 executive committee members were elected on the spot. All expenses will be decided by the executive committee. The office will be located within the West City Business Community Federation, and meetings will be held once a week. The meeting adjourned at 5:00 PM.

The merchants in the area of Chen Ying Shi Ta Nan continued to hold a meeting. The merchants in the area of Chen Ying Shi Nan Ba on Zhonghua and Fangxie Roads were forced to collect rent by Zhuang Xianghe, who hired lawyer Wang Chengkuan, because they had asked for rent reduction. Therefore, the shops continued to hold a meeting the night before to discuss countermeasures. All attendees were present. Cao Mo was publicly elected as the chairman. He reported that the previous letter from all the tenants requesting the landlord to reduce the rent had expired, but he was still ignoring it. They discussed how to deal with it. The agreed methods were: (1) The landlord's failure to respond is equivalent to tacitly agreeing to the rent reduction, which can also be used as evidence in law. (2) According to the reports of the tenants, the landlord privately persuaded the other seven tenants, willing to reduce the rent by 10%, but not willing to cooperate with Cao. The rent reduction is a whole issue, not an issue of individuals. It should be denied to avoid the landlord's alienation and sabotage of unity. (3) The tenants are willing to sign a covenant of alliance to express their determination. If there is a violation, they are willing to accept punishment. (4) If the landlord is not sincere in reducing the rent, they will deposit the rent due in the Shanghai City Bank from now on. (5) The legal advisor, lawyer Li Ming, will reply to lawyer Wang Chengkuan, detailing the reasons for not paying the rent. (6) Participate in the West City Business Community Rent Reduction Promotion Conference in its entirety. (7) Set aside 10% of the original rent as funds for negotiations. (8) Issue a declaration announcing that the landlord is oppressing the tenants and collecting excessive rent, and ask for assistance from all walks of life. The above methods were discussed and the meeting adjourned at 10:00 PM.
