Bombay Cotton Industry Weekly Report

Last week's market activity was largely due to speculators focusing on the April/May period in anticipation of the August 21st estimate release. Japanese demand was moderate, Shanghai was selling futures, European news was slightly weak, and new cotton was generally being shipped to Lancashire. Local factories were paying attention to spot goods. The Lihou rain activity was due to inland coastal rain erosion, which slightly damaged Bai Luoxi. In terms of rainfall, it was not yet excessive. According to reliable estimates, the area of the Cotu cotton field has increased by 10% compared to last year. Unfavorable News for New US Cotton

New York, August 3rd telegram reporting the cotton market conditions for the week, early in the week, unfavorable weather and poor cotton production news caused futures cotton to rise sharply, but it soon rebounded as many parties settled and the European situation became worrisome again. It is uncertain whether private estimates of poor cotton production are accurate, and the cotton production outlook may be overly discounted. This is also why merchants are shifting towards the selling side. Trading gradually decreased, and many in the industry squared their trades to await the USDA cotton production report. It is reported that storms in the Gulf of Mexico have caused considerable damage to southern Texas, but it has benefited cotton production elsewhere. Northern Texas, Oklahoma, and parts of Arkansas are still suffering from drought. According to recent news from Washington, the Penhale Act will be implemented even if cotton receipts are below the limit, but efforts are being made to allow cotton farmers whose cotton production is lower than their previous limit to sell excess cotton exceeding the tax-free amount to farmers whose cotton production exceeds the limit. The delay in issuing tax-free certificates has prevented new cotton from the Southwest from entering the market sooner.

Piece Goods

Woolen Fabric Autumn Sales Gradually Start

Woolen fabric piece goods, autumn sales are also about to start. As the new autumn approaches, merchants in the market are starting to prepare one after another, and the standard market is entering a better situation. Yesterday, merchants from Chengdu and Chongqing and Shenzhuang's were strongly interested in thick woolen camel hair fabrics. Merchants from Beijing, Tianjin, and Hankou mostly came to Shanghai to select and purchase goods themselves. There were inquiries and negotiations for various popular Western-style goods. This is the first batch of business in the second half of the year. Formal large-scale transactions will need to wait another half a month. Looking at the atmosphere at the meeting yesterday, apart from winter goods not yet being formally standardized, autumn woolen fabrics, mainstream goods seem to be better than Western-style goods.

Miscellaneous

Arrival of Opening Four Meter Goods Causes a Steep Decline

Wool and cotton thread prices have fallen sharply recently because since the tariff reduction, a large number of Japanese "opening four meter" goods have been imported and have arrived in large quantities. Each item has fallen by as much as thirty or forty yuan. A double-strand of 32 counts now sells for only 565 yuan per piece. All wool weaving factories are even more weakened because supply exceeds demand. This shipment was sold by brokerage firms.

Silk and Tea

US Initiates International Silk Industry Conference

丨China is Also Among Those Invited丨

American silk merchants recently organized the International Raw Silk Association in New York and scheduled an International Silk Industry Conference. They sent telegrams inviting representatives from silk-producing countries to participate. China also received a telegram invitation from the association. The Silk Improvement Committee organized by the Economic Committee is paying close attention to the association. In addition to replying to the association expressing agreement, they have telegraphed the Chinese consulate in New York, requesting them to send someone to attend the meeting and to investigate and report back the association's objectives and details at any time for review.

Yellow and White Reeled Silk Prices Continue to Fall

Local silk factories, due to excessive losses and inability to support operations, are preparing to shut down, and the wages owed to female workers must be cleared. They can only sell the silk they have on hand at a loss. Chinese and foreign silk merchants are taking the opportunity to suppress prices, exacerbating the silk market's downturn. Yesterday, 50 bales of white reeled silk and 10 bales of yellow reeled silk were received from Choumen and Dachang, respectively, and prices continued to weaken.

Rayon Remains Firm

The rayon market situation recently, the local sales market is still light, the Japanese goods with 30 count number one body is improved yesterday, each case 390 yuan, not tax the sale price is 185 yuan each case, so the purchaser are happy to adopt, in addition to the goods remain solid and hard

Shanghai Silk Factories Closing Reaches Five

There are a total of thirty-three silk factories in Shanghai that have started reeling new cocoons. However, since the beginning of summer, each silk factory has had excessive losses and cannot maintain production and had to temporarily stop operation, as of yesterday, the total number of silk factories that have been forced to stop operation in the city are Yingfeng, Gongyi, Jiyu, Fuxing and Yutong, with a total of more than 2,000 silk looms idle, about half of them will be closed by the end of this month. They are now rushing to reel the remaining dry cocoons in order to pay off the wages owed to female workers separately.

Tea Market Quiet Due to Holiday

Yesterday was the Western merchants' summer holiday, and major British foreign firms closed their offices as usual. Some dealers only had half-day transactions, resulting in an unusually quiet tea market. The only firms in the city that purchased Qimen and Ningzhou black tea, and Luzhuang Zhenmei, Zhenmei, Gongxi, and Hamu green tea, were Xiehe, Tianxiang, Tianyu, and Fushi, totaling over 1,300 boxes. These were mostly goods negotiated last week, so there was not much change in tea prices.

Increases by 1.5 Jiao

Dutch red goods arriving in the first ten days of next month continued to open yesterday, priced at 2.75 Dutch guilders, new regulations excluding tax.

Shanghai Shenbao Local Supplement

Talk

The Power of Modern Women

— Qiong Sheng

This year is the Women's National Products Year, and it seems that these mediocre women should devote their patriotic enthusiasm to buying national products. However, in reality, it is unexpected. Recently, the International Trade Bureau announced that the import of women's cosmetics such as rouge and perfume in China has reached 850,000 in half a year, which is nearly more than last year's 1.5 million, and there is a trend of "later overtaking". In June alone, the import of perfume and rouge reached 70,334 gold units, equivalent to 144,044 yuan in national currency; and the number of lace for fashionable women's clothing was even more surprising, with a total of 577,962 yuan in national currency imported in six months of this year.

No wonder many people admire modern women not only for their enchanting power, but also for their economic "power." It is worth remembering that not long ago, because women generally liked to go barefoot in summer and did not wear stockings or silk stockings, the business of several sock factories in this city suddenly declined, so they sent a letter to the Chamber of Commerce to forward it to the Executive Yuan to ban women's bizarre costumes in order to get relief. The slightest decoration and clothing of women can make the market sluggish and cause a huge leak in the country's foreign trade. How can this not be said that women have great economic "power"!

Indeed, some modern women's socks are related to the prosperity and decline of the market and the country's financial plan, which is indeed an economic power; but looking at its essence through a "Western mirror", it is not the luck of modern women. Because the current depression of all industries has reached the point of "getting worse", while women's beauty and appearance are "getting better", this is definitely not the result of shouting "equality between men and women" and "women's economic independence" in recent years, but a living drama of selling oneself for glory and dancing on foreign coins.

Economic panic reduces the production of the entire society, which in turn lowers the status of women. This has become the root cause of the unique prosperity of some women who are afraid of not being fashionable, while most people are standing on tiptoe, working hard. Because most women nowadays admire "Su Ji Zi's wealth and gold", and those who can wear skirts and cloth hairpins and "weep in a cow clothing" are really hard to find even if they break their straw shoes. This makes friends living in "small rooms" break the illusion of "Scholar Zhang", and what appears in women's eyes is that only rich and young people can become a happy son-in-law of "naked belly on the east bed". However, in order to tie the hearts of such men, many women have to compete for the exquisiteness of decoration. Those who are waiting for a price to be estimated want to pursue it, and those who already have a home need to be stable, and for many who are involved in the "social" field, decoration has become their profession. As this trend arrives, foreign rouge and Parisian perfume have become necessities for women that "cannot be separated for a moment". This is why the number of cosmetics imported is so alarming, and the reason why it cannot be saved is equal to the fact that women have to be modern in order to sell themselves. Regardless of how beautiful the propaganda of "Women's National Products Year" and "promoting national products" sounds, it cannot change the habit of women using dressing as a marketing tool.

Therefore, this kind of economic "power" of women is actually a power crawling under the economy. Rather than saying that it can enable women to achieve equality between men and women, it is better to say that it increases the nature of women being played with. Many women who are fortunate enough to be displayed at fashion exhibitions, please put down your arrogant psychology of looking down on everything and think about the objective significance of this situation.

Returning Home at Night

— Feng

Treading on the moonlight, with a sad heart, I returned from my aunt's house. I like walking at night. The bright moon hangs over my head, trampling on my own shadow, listening to the chirping of insects in the fields, as if I were in a precious painting, walking forward on the path. Occasionally, a few barks of dogs in the distance are like black shadows shaking in front of that thatched cottage. If it is a full moon, the wind blows the rice waves, and my steps become light and elegant, and my courage is so great. Especially in summer, I am disturbed by mosquitoes at night and cannot sleep soundly. Although the people living together are enjoying the cool in the courtyard, I hate them, I hate them for endlessly telling stories that people do not want to hear, or talking bad about the east family and the west family. In fact, our courtyard is quite large, with a flowered wall on three sides and some miscellaneous flowers planted, but it is already very precious in the countryside. In the middle, there are three pots of lotus flowers, and bursts of fragrance come to the nose with the wind, which can also invigorate people's spirits. In such a quiet environment, you can each drag a chair and sit on the four sides, waving the palm fan in your hand at will, or looking up at the clear moon without a cloud, how leisurely and洒脱. Those weaving girls鳴時時時時花在花中時鳴時歇,彷彿音樂 music, we should lean ears to listen, the fatigue of the day, at this time forgot to clean. However, as soon as you step into the courtyard in front of the window, it is like entering a traveling theater. I often turn around and go for a walk in the fields alone. I like walking at night and this has become a habit.

This morning, a servant from my aunt's house came to ask me to go, saying that my cousin had returned home for summer vacation. I grew up in my aunt's house, and my aunt is like my mother. My cousin is five years older than me, and she treats me, this younger brother, like her own brother. My aunt also made a joke, saying that Yu Jie would be your wife, but this is an impossible fact. We only know "to be good", and know other things. Later, as I grew older, I seemed to fall in love with my cousin. At that time, I went to Shanghai to study, and after we separated, we became estranged when we met. In fact, each other's age is also the reason for the estrangement. I can only have admiration for my cousin.

Last year, she got married, and I had a small exam at school. My aunt wrote several letters, but I couldn't return home once. To this day, I still seem to be unable to let go of this matter. Now that I am on summer vacation at home, I went to her house at noon. My aunt still patted me on the shoulder and touched my face when she saw me. She was very happy that I graduated this year and asked me if I would go to university. My cousin was thin, and she avoided me when she saw me.

In the afternoon, I went fishing in the back river alone. The peach tree that we planted by hand in the beginning has already blossomed and borne fruit. Remembering that life is like morning dew, I really want to cry. At this time, my aunt ran over and sat by the river. She talked from afar, talking about my cousin, saying that her husband was dissolute, gambled, and prostituted, a bad guy who did everything. My cousin repeatedly advised him not to listen, and was so angry that he became ill, and his words were sad. I listened in a daze, and the fishing rod almost slipped out of my hand.

After dinner, my cousin asked me in a low voice to go for a cool air. I followed her to the courtyard without hesitation. It was like my home there, with many people sitting in a noisy manner. When they saw my cousin, they hurriedly gave up their seats and chatted. We couldn't say a word to each other.

I said goodbye and came out. My aunt asked me to stay overnight. I didn't answer, and my cousin watched me off at the gate of the courtyard. Treading on the moonlight, with a sad heart, I returned from my aunt's house. The tranquility of the fields no longer aroused my interest, and I bowed my head to miss the equally sad heart over there!

Fantasy

— Jue Fu

Fantasy is similar to dreaming. No matter who it is, they will inevitably have moments of wild thoughts in their minds; however, because these thoughts are mostly related to their own fame and fortune, it is rare to express them in words and tell others nakedly.

Now, I will break the rule and talk about a little bit of my fantasy here.

For several months, I have often thought this way: I am a person who makes a living by writing. Even if I am blessed by God, I can earn thirty or twenty yuan a month to live on. I am confined to my residence all day long, eating, sleeping, reading, and writing. Even if I live to be a hundred years old, how much stuff can I come up with? Moreover, the scope of life is so narrow, and no matter how many topics are changed, they will never come up with a new pattern; for example, flowers, moons, cold, heat, poverty, suffering, ... are these things not often seen at the pen tips of ordinary people all year round? If the topics are used up one day, and you have to eat, then you have no choice but to plagiarize and copy other people's things, or specialize in fabricating facts and peeking at the small loopholes in someone's articles to use as your own writing material. What is the meaning of living like this?

"The way of life must be changed, whether it is being an official, farming, doing business, being a hired worker, ..." I feel this deeply; however, I have neither the ability of a sharp-pointed trowel, nor

Page 18

no large amount of capital, or a close relationship with a rich businessman or a big official, so naturally I can't be an official, and I can't do business; as for farming and being a hired worker, I naturally can't realize it if I don't have three or five acres of fertile land, strong arms, and a tall body. Thinking repeatedly, I can't think of a better way to go. In the end, I don't know how, but I even thought of walking all over the country on foot. I thought that, like a tramp, begging from one township to another, from one town to another, if my life does not starve to death, freeze to death, or be killed by wild beasts and robbers, I would go into the rural areas that have suffered from natural and man-made disasters for many years, see how the hard-working and frugal old farmers look, climb over mountains above five thousand feet, taste the taste of the cold winter night sky, walk along the river and lake under the sunset, go deep into the verdant forests, majestic and dangerous valleys, ... see what the scenery there is like, After three or five years, it will not be in vain for a person who loves literature to taste hardship! Although, in the present China, it is not easy to realize this desire for a poor person, even if he travels on foot; however, if you are willing to risk your life, there may be a little hope of realizing it.

I very much hope that this little fantasy of mine can be realized. I don't know if there is anyone else who has the same idea and is willing to be my travel companion?

P.S. I plan to realize this wish of mine around September 10th. If anyone also loves this way and is willing to be a companion, please send a letter to He Juefu, Fudan University, so that we can make an appointment to discuss it further.

Sharing Watermelon—Thoughts on Eating Watermelon—

Hometown

— A Ping

I was awakened by the alarm clock at five o'clock. I raised my head and looked at the bed opposite, and my brother was also looking at me with a smile. This seems to have become a habit. I put my feet on the ground and hurriedly opened the window, letting the stale air from the previous night be replaced by fresh air. I took a deep breath against the window, and my hands waved in a way that was not at all regular; however, this is not the training ground, and there is no physical education teacher shouting one, two, three, so no matter how much you mess around, it is hygienic.

I rinsed my mouth and washed my face with cold water, and sometimes I wiped my upper and lower body. The two brothers took the teapot and went out. In front of the door is a shallow stream, and several willows are planted by the stream, whispering to the water from time to time with the morning breeze. The cicadas are already making noise on the treetops, knowing and knowing, do you know that autumn is coming, and your life is short in a moment?

Standing on the wooden bridge, I stared at the school of fish in the stream, they were so lively competing for the food floating on the water. After a while, they hid in the bottom of the river, like a shy virgin. Here, there is never a trace of fishermen, and they live their lives in逍遥自在.

Walking forward along the river bank on the opposite bank, the thatched huts are all familiar faces, and a smile is a greeting. They can't say "Good morning, sir!" The clothes from the night before are busy washing, and today's meal has to be cooked before sunrise, so when we return, they have already gone to the market town to do business.

I don't know when a little black dog followed us. Grabbing its front paws and wagging its tail, it was very affectionate. The dogs in the countryside are so cute. Although they will jump up and bark a few times when they see strangers, they don't hope to sit in a car, eat milk biscuits, and if they drop a little white rice, they will guard your door every day.

To the teahouse, this tea house is also three thatched huts. One is the tea seat, one is the residence of the shop owner, they are a couple and a twelve-year-old son, and the other is selling soy milk in the morning and snacks in the afternoon, and also running all kinds of Beijing groceries: however, as long as you say the name of the shop, Lao Wanxing, everyone in the neighborhood knows and understands. Many letters are forwarded from here every day. At this time, there are already several tea customers with their upper bodies exposed and their legs bare in the tea seat, and they are all familiar faces.

"Three officials, five officials, good morning!" Taking the teapot, giving four copper coins, Lao Wanxing always says this sentence.

"Busy!" is our answer.

It has become a habit to say this every day, but it is not annoying, and both sides feel very 친절한; or it is because of the straightforwardness of the country people.

Taking the bean curd and returning the same way, the big sun has already探起 from the east, and the dewdrops on the weeds along the way are shining. The little boat of the fisherman who touches the fish has just rowed out, and the old Li with white hair must be smiling and saying: "I will go to hear Da Hongpao again tonight, and I will break the White Sparrow Temple."

My hand tightened, and his boat shot like an arrow from behind us.

Lao Wanxing's teahouse always invites a running dockworker to talk about cause and effect every summer, and five copper coins can listen for an hour. It is very crowded every night, and some people bring their own benches. There is nothing to do in the countryside, and they come to listen every night and become addicted.

Returning home, the whole family has gotten up. We move all the flowers in the yard to the study, which is also a hobby of our two brothers. But when it comes to flowers, it is really embarrassing, they are all those balsam, cockscomb and so on. Later, we asked for a few wax reds, which have been regarded as precious flower species.

Last night, I read my fifth brother's letter under the lamp. He said that my beloved single-braided wax red withered, and the old Li, who was more than sixty years old, was caught and died in prison for only one night because of the field rent. He was a bachelor, and the neighbors collected money to buy a coffin and bury him. He said that the teahouse will not invite anyone to talk about cause and effect this year, and there is nothing to do at night. He hopes that the newspapers and magazines that I have read will be sent to him a little every week...

I didn't sleep well all night last night, and even the accordion next door became a novice, so annoying.

Soviet Youth's Flying Game (Part 1)

— (Moscow Correspondent Yin Yuan)

(1) Parachute Jump

An airplane slowly rotates above the green airplane field. The huge humming sound emitted by the airplane is not very clear to the people near the huge (I) character. This airplane, seen from below, looks like a carnivorous bird with its wings spread. On one of the wings, a tiny shadow crawled out of the cabin, jumped down, and plunged headfirst into the void. The attention of the audience below is focused on this tiny shadow floating in the air.

"Has this thing opened or not?" In the instant after this figure fell, a large umbrella opened on his body, and the shadow hung under the umbrella and gradually fell to the ground. This parachute shone a rainbow in the bright sunshine and swayed down steadily. The shadow of this parachute jump can already be identified in the clear half-sky. Finally, it landed, and the parachute swaying in the wind opened above his head like a tent. He quickly took the umbrella and packed it up.

At this time, the crowd rushed forward and shouted: "How is it?"

"Very good, I came down very smoothly," the man replied, pretending to be calm, to replace his smug pride. Such pride is deserved and allowed. This is an unforgettable day, the day of his first parachute jump, and now he has the right to hang the green badge of the parachute jump on his chest, which is a badge of courage and skill.

Underground

— Yi

It's about five o'clock. The stars in the sky are vaguely blurred, and the fish-white light gradually appears on the eastern horizon. In the fields, on the grasslands, and in the jungles, countless sparrows are flying. The flowing water in the small river glistens under the morning light, and the black shadows covering the mountains, forests, and plains have dissipated. Dawn, this quiet and peaceful dawn has come to the world.

The long and strange cry of the steam whistle awakened the people in the villages and tile houses near and far in the mountains and forests. They know that this is the signal of the arrival of dawn, and the time for them to start operating every day has come.

The chimneys on the tile houses began to release wisps of white smoke. Women and children are doing their housework, and strong men are all taking up the tools of their work—gas lamps and small iron hoes—and heading towards the mine. On the small paths of the plain, rows of them seem to be a marching army.

On that hillside, on the four sides of the railway, workers are everywhere. The wheels are rumbling, and the elevators are spitting out groups of tired and panting workers from the depths of the ground, thousands of feet or hundreds of feet below, and newly sucking in groups of energetic people.

They, leaving the natural world, the resting place of mankind at dawn, are sent to this world thousands of feet or hundreds of feet below the ground for the sake of life. There is no sun, no sky, no mountains, and no rivers. It is just gloomy, full of dirty and wet mud, and dark all around with stench and coal dust. This is another world, another human world.

The whistle of the steam whistle cannot be heard, and people's laughter cannot be heard. Filling the underground is some breathing, exertion, and the slight sound of walking. Occasionally, a loud sound is the sound of the coal seam collapsing. In this sound, some people will lose their lives.

Leaving nature, leaving the human world, in this deep underground, there are tens of thousands of people working all day long. They lost the guarantee of life, lost the light of the sun, sold their strength and lives for the sake of life, and worked forever in this underground.

Novel

One Night (6) Li Huaiying

The other four welcomed her as if they were receiving a warrior who had returned victoriously from the battlefield. They shouted in unison and gathered around the table. Mrs. Zheng's two daughters, one eleven years old and the other nine years old, were originally playing in the alley. When they saw Mrs. Xing buying wine, they guessed that there would be something to eat, which moved their little appetites, so they followed and ran in.

"Why aren't you playing? What are you doing here?"

Mrs. Zheng questioned her two children sternly when she saw them. Her intention was not to let the children watch them drink. She wanted to drive the two children out and then said:

"Go out and play!"

The children didn't leave. They didn't want to go back outside empty-handed. Mrs. Liu saw the children's eyes fixed on these things and saw their little demands. She grabbed a handful of peanuts and sent the two children away.

"Let's drink."

Mrs. Xing suggested. When she said this, she seemed to have made a great determination, and her face was wrinkled tightly.

Mrs. Ning said with a smile:

"How can we drink without glasses?"

"Do you still need a glass? Why be so polite! If you don't need a glass, can't you drink directly from the bottle?"

Mrs. Sun said fiercely, as if she was angry with someone.

That's what they did. The corks of the three bottles were opened one after another, and the five of them passed them around and drank.

Except for Mrs. Zheng and Mrs. Chuang, who had a three-cup capacity, the remaining three had never let their lips touch a wine glass on weekdays. This time, they were desperate to drink to relieve their sorrows.

The wine was sweet, the heart was bitter, and the tears were salty. They poured it in, burned it, and flowed it out. Gradually, their faces turned red, their mouths were dry, and their heads were heavy.

"I don't believe we should starve to death!"

"Xinjiang, what kind of place is Xinjiang? Why don't people go to fight Japan in that place, but fight among themselves?..."

"Let's get drunk, let's get drunk, it's better to get through this day."

Drinking and talking, gradually, some people felt that the people in front of them began to sway, and the house was also spinning. Mrs. Xing, Mrs. Ning, and Mrs. Sun dropped their wine bottles and fell on the bed, with saliva foaming at the corners of their mouths. After vomiting for a while, they vomited a large pile of food, which flowed all over their faces and beds. Mrs. Zheng and Mrs. Liu originally wanted to help them, but they fell on the bed unconsciously.

The whole house was filled with a strong smell of alcohol.

The night is deep, the night is deep.

Mrs. Zheng's two children walked upstairs singing songs. They were ready to go to bed. A little cat sneaked into the house from somewhere before them. It sniffed around the house with its inspired nose for a while, and then quietly sneaked out again. (End)

Announcement The author's original intention in writing this novel was only to make the world understand the plight of the anti-Japanese relatives in Shanghai. There was no malice. Yesterday, I heard from my friend Mr. Li that I realized that it caused a misunderstanding and was considered to be intentionally insulting. This was due to not understanding the author's original intention. I hereby declare and apologize. Li Huaiying respectfully

Shenbao Local Supplement Movie Special

A HOLLYWOOD WIFE'S CONFESSION (PART TWO)

— MI QI

The Difficulty of Being a Famous Movie Star's Wife: Please Read Carefully to Understand the Truth

Later, we moved into a large house with eighteen rooms, complete with gardens, a swimming pool, a tennis court, and so on. But in many ways, it felt like a prison. What was the point of such a hollow place? Todd was always busy, rarely having time to be with me. Thankfully, he adored our children. That was at least somewhat comforting. Once, on Christmas Eve, we held a party at our house. Our guests arrived one by one. We had just come downstairs when we overheard someone among the guests asking, "Did you know about Freeland and Sylvia Sheila's affair? I wonder how Freeland's wife feels?" Suddenly, they saw us and became extremely embarrassed. I leaned on the railing, pretending to be nonchalant, and laughed, "She's furious! She's so angry that she eats children like you for breakfast every morning!" With that, a small storm passed. Everyone raised their eyebrows, as if saying "Oh," but the atmosphere calmed down, though my feet were ice cold. That night, after the guests left, Todd hugged me and kissed the tip of my ear, saying, "You truly are an impenetrable fortress." He only said those words, but I felt it was the closest thing we'd had in months.

Later, the company boss wanted to send him on a trip to the Midwest and East Coast. I accompanied him. When we set off, I felt it was the happiest day since Todd became a star. However, that joy was fleeting. When we arrived at San Bernardino, it all dissipated. He was reading a news item aloud with me… when suddenly four girls! As delicate as rosebuds! Burst into our compartment. Their glittering eyes were full of adoration. Their luscious red lips trembled with emotion. I believe they didn't even notice me. Todd signed his name on their books for each of them; patted one of their hands for something she said; then dismissed them. From that moment on, I could never return to my former self. Suddenly, I felt an indescribable weariness. I thought, even if I had the strength to fight one woman and keep my husband, how could I fight all the women in the world? But it felt like that was exactly what I had to do. Women came in droves to surround him. At one stop, Todd was helping me off the train, but a woman pulled his arm and dragged him away. I didn't see him again for two hours. He ran to the hotel, saw me, and laughed, "Look at me, don't I look like a scarecrow made of souvenirs?" I took a closer look, and it was true. His bow tie was gone, his collar was torn, and the buttons on his clothes had all vanished. At the next stop, it was even worse. Many policemen protected him as he disembarked. Entering and exiting theaters also required the special protection of the police. One evening, we were in the inn, exhausted after a hard day. Todd cradled my chin and kissed me like a child. Ah! It had been so long since that had happened. I thought I had finally won. Suddenly, behind us came a long "Ah..." Two women laughed and popped out, having snuck in and hidden behind the sofa. I felt like I didn't have any private time anymore. He belonged to every woman...

In the end, I didn't accompany Todd back to Hollywood, because the company had an urgent matter that required him to return, and my sister was ill and needed me to take care of her. Thus, we were separated for another two months. On the day I returned, Todd threw a grand party for me at home. Big names and stars walked in and out of our house, wearing out the doorsteps. I was happy, but extremely tired, only hoping they would leave early so that Todd and I could rest and be intimate. That night, after two o'clock, the guests left, and as I was unpacking my luggage, he said to me, "Darling, I'm so sorry. But it's all over. I can't go on like this forever." I asked, "Are you talking about Sylvia?" He said, "No. It's Janice Morgan." Janice Morgan! A middle-aged woman, known as America's greatest seductress! Many people had committed suicide for her. Of course, Todd wasn't willing to mention divorce. Mentioning divorce would be detrimental to his career, and might even ruin Janice's.

My only hope now is that one day, Todd will change his mind and return to me. We still attend parties, film screenings, and press previews as usual. My job is to stand at the door beside my husband, showing ourselves off to everyone passing by; and I must wear that content smile… The purpose is to silence all rumor-mongers. But when no one is watching, I slip away, go out the back door and go home… alone. Wife? No! I am a half-dead, numb, soulless phantom. I am just a windbreak for a big Hollywood star." (The End)

Movie Reviews

REVIEW OF "THE FAITHFUL HEART"

— LUO PING

ONCE TO EVERY WOMAN

丨CATHAY FILM

"The Faithful Heart," like "It Happened One Night," is based on a story from Cosmopolitan magazine. However, there is a significant difference between A. J. Cronin and S. H. Adams. At the very least, Cronin's serious approach to creation in "The Faithful Heart" is worth our attention.

"The Faithful Heart" shares some similarities with "Remedy for Love," both demanding that doctors be conscientious about life and fulfill their duty to save humanity.

Here, it curses the derelict and selfish doctors, satirizes the arrogant and jealous head of surgery, and denounces the callous nurses who lack compassion for patients.

It depicts the love of an old married couple who are sometimes fighting and sometimes loving. The pain of a dancer whose face is disfigured by acid, sacrificing in a capitalist society, the deep affection between a young, poor, and sick couple who say to the doctor, "Saving her is saving my youth," and these descriptions are all very light, delicate, vivid, and truthful. We can see the director's cleverness here.

The subjective opinion of the playwright of "The Faithful Heart" demands that doctors and nurses be conscientious about life and fulfill their duty to save "humanity," although the term "humanity" is still problematic. We acknowledge that the playwright's opinion is acceptable.

However, we also know that the demands of the playwright of "The Faithful Heart" cannot be separated from the demands of overall social reform, but Cronin has not understood this point. His fantasy is only to have these two doctors and nurses who fulfill their duty to save "humanity" be perfectly united under the existing social system, which cannot be said to be shortsighted.

The achievements of "The Faithful Heart," the contributions of director Lambert Hillyer and screenwriter Jo Swerling, cannot be denied. The handling is very economical, smooth, and crisp. Especially the handling of the section where the patient is undergoing surgery, the tense work in the room, the rapid expansion and contraction of the breathing ball, the descent of the measuring table and the rapid breathing sound, the panicked situation of the observers on the roof and the anxious inner description of the patient's husband tightly grasping the curtains in the next room, are like ten thousand tons of lead and iron tightly pressing on the audience's breath.

The actors are all average. Fay Wray and Walter Byron are the best, but Ralph Bellamy, who plays Burke, is a little lacking.

In the midst of the demands for realism in film, this film, which touches on some truth and is relatively satisfactory, is commendable.

"HELL'S HIGHWAY"丨丨Nanjing Screening JEckoakie the telephone worker

"NEW WOMAN" DIRECTOR IS REFRESHED

Although "New Woman," one of Lianhua's major productions this year, has not yet started filming, audiences who care about Lianhua's productions have long known that it is a great work of triple stars: Sun Shiyi writing the script, Cai Chusheng directing, and Ruan Lingyu starring. Because Director Cai demanded that everything about his new work be new, he had been working day and night for more than twenty days to use his agile brain, to the point where he almost became an "old man," unkempt and unshaven. But now he has solved all the difficult problems he was thinking about, so he has restored his original appearance, refreshed, and radiant, still a young man in his prime.

"THE BIG ROAD" INSPECTION TEAM RETURNS LOADED

Lianhua's major production, Sun Yu's new work "The Big Road," returned safely to Shanghai on the evening of the sixth day after the organization of the inspection team set off for the Hangzhou-Huizhou Road for location shooting. This trip covered more than three thousand three hundred miles, with footprints all over the two provinces. Everyone who returned was happy and returned with a full load: what they had in common was that the magnificent, majestic, winding, secluded scenery along the way gave them unexpected gains; what they had separately was that Factory Director Lu and Director Sun picked up countless colorful, crystal-clear small stones in the mountain streams of Huangshan, Qiu Yiwei's camera pre-loaded with beautiful negatives, and Meng Junmou carried a large bag of famous Huizhou fruits.

GUIDELINES FOR SUBMISSIONS TO THE SHEN BAO FILM SUPPLEMENT

This publication is a film publication to assist in the cultural promotion of art. We welcome external contributions and pay generously upon publication.

Once the text is published and paid for, the copyright belongs to Shen Bao.

The text in this publication is mainly in vernacular Chinese and must use modern punctuation. If the submission is a translation, it should include the original work. Avoid mixing in English where possible.

Do not write on both sides of the manuscript paper or write horizontally, and do not use a pencil.

Due to the limited space in this publication, the text should be as concise as possible, with each manuscript limited to approximately 500 characters.

When submitting, each article must be stamped with a seal, otherwise it will not be compensated.

This publication is not responsible for the preservation or return of texts, photographs, etc., unless prior notice is given and return postage is attached.

Submissions that are submitted to multiple publications, copied texts, or copied explanations will not be compensated after being rejected.

Film Novel

A GOOD SON AND A GOOD WIFE (BORN TO BE KISSED) (9)

— XIN ZHI

This place is really like a palace, Edie thought. Looking up at the high ceilings and down at all the luxurious furnishings, it was so lovely. They walked to a wing room, which Pan Qi said was his son's private room, a place where others were not allowed to go. Edie heard this and felt happy in her heart, so she strolled in and ran to the balcony, overlooking the shimmering water below. Pan Qi saw her go in and whispered to his son, "You must go to Washington by the end of this week. You go figure it out." After he finished speaking, he walked away. Edie turned around and saw that only Tom was left, so she asked curiously, "Where's your father?" Tom said, "He went to check the luggage." He casually picked up a photo album and handed it to Edie to look at. Edie flipped through it and saw a small photo inside, a child, held by a nanny, smiling widely. Edie asked, "Is this you?" Tom nodded and said, "I think you must have been very pretty when you were little." He looked at her as if he loved her very much. Edie said, "Unfortunately, I can't prove it. My family is very poor and doesn't have money for photos." She then told Tom about her family. Her father's story, her mother's story..., and even her encounter and engagement with Chris, she revealed everything. She even showed Tom the ring on her hand. After hearing what she had to say, Tom's heart felt something, so he stared at her blankly, without saying a word. After a while, Edie slowly said, "Your father doesn't like me." Tom said, "Of course he likes you very much. You are the first of my girlfriends that he has invited home." After a while, he took her hand again and said, "Don't worry. Come on. There are still many places you haven't seen yet." He opened a door, and inside was a bedroom. She went in to take a look and couldn't help but admire it.

The sound of a car startled her. She climbed to the window and looked out. A car was parked below her, with luggage piled in the front, and Pan Qi was sitting in the back, leaving. Edie couldn't help but yell, "Pan Qi is crazy!" Pan Qi waved his hand with a smile and said, "Edie, goodbye!" Edie turned around and said angrily to Tom, "This is what you did, isn't it?" Tom said, "Hey, we haven't been alone together yet." Edie said, "Of course not! Don't even think about it! I'm going home!" She turned the doorknob, but the door wouldn't open. Edie said angrily to Tom, "Open the door quickly." Tom said sharply, "Honey, you don't have to be angry." Edie blushed and scolded, "You are such a heartless person. Bringing me to this place, making fun of me for not having a big house on Pike Street, making fun of me for not having a powerful family to back me up!" Tom said, "I don't want to do anything to you..." Edie shouted, "Of course you can't do anything to me! I'm not afraid of you either! I've encountered this kind of thing before! I can protect myself!" Tom looked amused and said, "Tell me! You adorable thing!" Edie continued, "You have always been able to get whatever you want, and you are satisfied, but you have not understood one thing, that you are not the only one who has feelings, other people have them too." She pulled her own hair and said, "My hair has color, that's right. I look a bit like a woman of questionable character, that's right. No one thinks of me as anything good, but I have never looked down on myself!" Her temples were trembling with anger. Tom said, "You don't need to coax me. Aren't you and I both living people!" Edie helplessly pleaded again, "Tom, please forgive me! Why won't you help me a little?" (To be continued)
